The Vienna Police Commissioner and the authorities have agreed that those who commit internal rebellion or treason may be executed using simplified procedures. All public roads are prohibited from gathering in groups. Shops, cafes, and taverns should all be closed at 8:00 p.m. This order will be implemented from July 26. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

The Course of Events in Vienna 49

Vienna: Austria underwent a major political upheaval today. The details that have come to light are as follows. At 1:00 PM, a number of National Socialist terrorists stormed the broadcasting studio of the Radio Verkehrs AG (the central radio station), aiming to cut off the wires connecting the broadcasting studio with the transmission station. At that time, one of the terrorists announced over the airwaves that the government had resigned, and thus the alarming news of the coup was transmitted everywhere via radio. The director of the Radio Verkehrs AG, Mr. Holder, was killed on the spot by the National Socialist Party members. When the police outside the radio station learned that an incident had occurred, they immediately surrounded the radio station and opened fire with machine guns into the building. At the same time, several bombs exploded inside the building, causing a fire to break out. Because the National Socialist Party members were all dressed in police uniforms, the police action was extremely difficult. By 2:00 PM, the transmission station of the central radio station had been restored to its original state, and the police attack on the broadcasting studio continued unabated. As a result, the sound of gunfire transmitted from the radio was clearly discernible. By 4:00 PM, the National Socialist Party members surrendered and were captured by the police. It is estimated that many National Socialist Party members died, and one policeman died. At that time, the streets were patrolled by police, and the government offices of the various ministries were occupied by federal troops, who set up machine guns. By 4:00 PM, a large contingent of federal troops had entered the Prime Minister's Office. Prime Minister Dollfuss, Minister of Public Security Fey, Secretary-General of the State Council Karwinsky, and others had been detained by National Socialist Party members inside the Prime Minister's Office. Communication between the Prime Minister's Office and the outside world was cut off from 2:00 PM. It was rumored that Dollfuss had been shot and wounded by National Socialist Party members, and that his injuries were quite serious. The National Socialist Party members, dressed in police uniforms, stormed into the Prime Minister's Office. It was heard that Prime Minister Dollfuss had

announced his intention to resign. In addition, it was heard that a large number of National Socialist Party members had gathered in the suburbs of Vienna, but the armed farmers of Lower Austria Province had also gathered to intervene and assist the government if necessary. After news of the resignation of the Stanz local government in Styria Province was released, 400 National Socialist Party members carrying firearms attacked the gendarmes on guard. One gendarme was shot and killed. At 3:00 PM, a patrolman in Innsbruck City was attacked and killed by two National Socialist Party members. The murderers were arrested on the spot. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

A Scene of the Tragedy of Mr. Tao's Death 50

(London) Yesterday morning at 11:30, when the cabinet was in session, the rebels began their activities. 150 members of the Austrian National Socialist Party, all dressed in police uniforms, gathered at the athletic club to finalize their plans. Then, they rushed to the room where the cabinet was meeting. Minister of Public Security and Minister of Interior Fey and his confidant, Deputy Minister of Defense Karwinsky, were immediately arrested. Prime Minister Tao had already left the room, but he was shot before he could get far. When Fey was taken to another room by a group of National Socialist Party members, "Little Napoleon" was lying on a sofa, barely breathing, with a bullet wound through his throat. Tao was only strong enough to speak a few words to his adjutant, murmuring, "Please take care of my family." After saying this, he breathed his last. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Minister of Public Security Fey reported today's incident on the radio, saying that Prime Minister Dollfuss was holding a State Council meeting, chairing the meeting himself. Suddenly, it was heard that members of the National Socialist Party, dressed in police uniforms, had sneaked into the office. They immediately stopped the meeting. However, the members of the National Socialist Party had already entered the room and detained Dollfuss, Fey, and Secretary-General Karwinsky. Then, they demanded a guarantee that they would not be punished and that they would be sent to the border before the cabinet members would be released. According to Acting Prime Minister Schuschnigg's estimation, a total of 144 rioters entered the Prime Minister's Office. After being surrounded by the military and police, they submitted a letter of surrender, requesting mediation by the German Ambassador to Austria. Furthermore, the new chief of detectives, Adam, described Dollfuss's final moments on the radio, saying that about a dozen rioters entered Dollfuss's office. The leader of the rioters saw Dollfuss and immediately fired two shots, both of which hit him in the chest. At that time, the servants in the room had been driven to other rooms, leaving only Dollfuss. After being shot, he ordered Fey to come forward and receive his last will. The rioters refused to allow a doctor to be summoned for treatment and refused to allow a pastor to perform the sacrament. At that point, Dollfuss breathed his last. In addition, the Vienna Daily reported that Dollfuss died at 4:30 PM. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Remembering Peace Until His Death 51

Vienna heard that Prime Minister Du had been shot in his right armpit and left ear. Although surgery with a rescue packet was performed, the thugs refused to provide medical assistance. The Prime Minister fell by the window, bleeding profusely and unconscious. After being slightly awake, he wanted to call a priest inside, but the rebels refused his request and only allowed him to meet with Minister of Public Security Fey for a few minutes. Du asked Fei to find a way to prevent unnecessary bloodshed. Du's last words were, "I only want peace and give my love to my wife and children", and he fainted and died at 3:45 pm. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Wife Heard the News and Rushed Back to Beijing for the Funeral 52

Mourning over the Corpse in Extreme Grief, Mrs. Dollfuss of Vienna and her two daughters returned to Beijing from Italy this afternoon to attend the funeral. They rushed to the Prime Minister's Office to see the body of her husband. President Miklas stood beside the corpse to offer condolences. The Prime Minister's widow mourned over the corpse and cried in extreme grief, and is still bowing her head in silent prayer beside the corpse. (National dispatch, 26th)

The body of Vienna Prime Minister Dollfuss has been moved from the scene of the incident to the conference table in his private office. The body is covered with a white cloth, behind which is a cross, with two candles placed next to it. Four iron helmet infantrymen are guarding the body with guns. Only relatives and friends are allowed into the inner room. The wounds are on the back, one on the neck, which is clearly visible. (National dispatch, 26th)

Minister of Education Temporarily Assumed the Post of Prime Minister 53

(London) At 10:00 pm last night, Minister of Education Dr. Schuschnigg officially announced the news of Prime Minister Dollfuss's death on the radio, and also announced that he had taken over the post of Acting Prime Minister. Mr. Xu said that the blood shed by Prime Minister Du will not be thrown into the empty bottle, and now the military and police are loyal to the government, and the government is capable of controlling the overall situation. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

President Refused to Compromise with the Traitors 54

(London) Fei Shaozuo and Ka Winsky were released and left the Presidential Palace. In the afternoon, the cabinet met and approved by President Miklas a resolution to refuse to contact the rebels. The cabinet had previously sent a large infantry team to the Prime Minister's Office, and a decision was made to continue to send a large team with orders that if the rebels refused to surrender, they would bombard the Prime Minister's Office.

When Fei Shaozuo was still imprisoned in the Prime Minister's Office, he wrote a letter to his colleagues, stating that the Prime Minister had been shot and injured, and that if bloodshed could be avoided, the Prime Minister would agree to any successor approved by President Miklas. However, the President resolutely refused to negotiate everything with the rebels. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Border Between Germany and Austria Blocked 55

(Berlin) After receiving news of the political turmoil in Austria, the German government ordered all border crossings to be blocked to prevent German National Social Party members or Austrian political exiles residing in Germany from sneaking into Austria. (National dispatch, 25th)

German Ambassador to Austria Recalled 56

(London) One important event after the turmoil in Austria is that Dr. Laze, the German ambassador to Austria, has now been recalled to Berlin. Mr. Lai was recalled for allowing the rebels to retreat into German territory without consulting his government. German Chancellor Hitler is now returning to Berlin from Berchtesgaden to assess the situation. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Condolences from Various Countries 57

Italian Prime Minister Lissoni Mussolini sent a telegram to Austrian Deputy Prime Minister Starhemberg today to condole the death of Prime Minister Du. The telegram said that Dr. Du died for the independence of Austria. During this very difficult period, Italy will continue to more effectively protect the principle of Austria's independence. He also said that Dr. Du and I had a very close personal relationship and shared the same political views. I am deeply saddened to hear the bad news. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

(London) According to news from Vienna, telegrams of condolence from various countries are still pouring in, including those from the Pope and President Hindenburg. Hindenburg's telegram was sent to Austrian President Mitzelas, expressing regret over the tragic death of Dr. Dollfuss. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

(Berlin) Foreign Minister Neurath went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs early this morning and sent a telegram to Vienna to formally express the German government's condolences for the death of Prime Minister Dollfuss. (National dispatch, 26th)

London, the British Emperor has today sent a telegram to Vienna to express his condolences. Foreign Secretary Simon expressed his condolences for the death of Dr. Dollfuss in the House of Commons today, and said that the attitude held by the United Kingdom is that Austria's independence must be maintained in accordance with the treaty. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Dollfuss Was an Outstanding Political Talent 58

Known Internationally as Little Napoleon, He Had Three Major Diplomatic Successes Vienna: Prime Minister Dollfuss was murdered by the National Socialists yesterday. Dollfuss was the youngest and smallest dictator in Europe, but his self-confidence and his brave, wise and ambitious talent were similar to Napoleon's. It was all Dollfuss's own strength that Austria was able to break away from the shackles of the Treaty of Saint-Germain and occupy a new place on the map of Europe. Dollfuss's success depended entirely on his ability to use international forces and domestic military, police and financial relations, but he claimed that it was all heavenly assistance. Dollfuss did not change his mind once he had made up his mind. It was not intentional stubbornness, but his determination came after much consideration and prayer. Whenever faced with difficult problems, he would go to church to pray for divine guidance, so although his attitude was firm, even his political enemies did not laugh at him. In May 1932, President Miklas ordered Dollfuss to form a cabinet. At that time, Dollfuss was the Minister of Agriculture. After receiving the order, the domestic political and economic situation worsened within a few months. After the dissolution of the parliament, Dollfuss took the post of dictator until now. Dollfuss had three major successes in the international community. The first was his efforts at the London World Economic Conference, the second was Austria's obtaining assistance from the League of Nations and issuing bonds in the United Kingdom, France, Italy, the Netherlands, Belgium, Sweden and other countries, and the third was his conflict with German Chancellor Hitler, which was intervened by the United Kingdom, France and Italy, who were deeply afraid of the merger of Germany and Austria, which Dollfuss was able to use. Dollfuss was also deeply opposed to the Jewish nation, but he never used violence to deal with them. (National dispatch, 26th)

News and Commentary from Various Nations 59

The Nazi Party Coup, Though Failed, Has Achieved Its Greatest Objective. The Times of London states that while the Nazi Party's coup has failed, it has achieved its greatest objective, namely the overthrow of the Dollfuss government. The newspaper also stated that it does not seem fair to hold Germany responsible for yesterday's riots in Vienna, but it is undeniable that the rebellion was caused by continuous incitement from the German side. (Reuter's dispatch, 26th)

Maintaining Austria's Independence is Tied to the Future of Peace in All of Europe. 60

(London) The Austrian incident came suddenly. British public opinion, after the initial shock, felt very uneasy. Coupled with the worrying tone of various newspapers, the anxiety has only deepened. The Daily Telegraph reported, "Yesterday's Austrian incident, its serious nature is self-evident. The impact it may have internationally is even more significant, as the independence of Austria is a matter of concern to the survival interests of all European countries." The Liberal Party's News Chronicle researches methods to guarantee European peace, saying, "Generally speaking, if European countries, and narrowly speaking, Austria's neighboring countries, can clearly express their determination to maintain international peace in response to this new situation, it would be of no small benefit to the new Austrian government." The Labour Party's Daily Herald believes that "Austria's Christian Pan-Germanism (i.e., the Christian Social Party led by Dollfuss) will not be able to hold power for long, and the Schuschnigg government will inevitably collapse soon." Looking at the above commentaries, the British Liberal and Labour newspapers have not yet forgiven Dollfuss for his suppression of the Socialists' uprising in February of this year, but the Conservative newspapers express admiration for Dollfuss's life with sympathy. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Ten Times More Serious Than the Assassination of the Austrian Heir, How Can the Great Powers Stand Idly By? 61

(London) Today, French and Italian newspapers commented on yesterday's incident in the Austrian capital, all criticizing Germany and advocating for the maintenance of Austrian independence. The Paris Figaro said that this crime was instigated by Germany, and how can Britain, France, and Italy turn a blind eye to this robbery? How can the League of Nations stand idly by? Austrian independence must be maintained. Le Journal stated that yesterday's incident in the Austrian capital was no different from the assassination of the Austrian heir in Sarajevo in the past, but the conflict is ten times greater than before. Le Petit Parisien said that international action cannot be taken immediately, but governments must maintain close contact. Italian newspapers said that guaranteeing the aspirations of the Italian people is not only what Austria wants, but also what the great powers should do.

(Reuter's dispatch, 26th)

Killing the Guarantor of Austria's Independence, Germany's Eastern Expansion Policy Initiated This 62

(Paris) After the news of the assassination of Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss arrived, it caused a great shock here. Newspapers expressed extreme indignation at the Nazi Party's means of killing "the guarantor of Austria's independence," feeling that such an incident should not be regarded merely as a sad state of internal instability. In reality, it is also the result of Germany's "eastern expansion" policy. The so-called eastern expansion policy, its first step is the realization of the merger of Germany and Austria. Newspapers also mentioned the attitude that the League of Nations and the three countries responsible for guaranteeing Austria's independence—Italy, England, and France—could adopt. Le Figaro reported, "Among all the impressions we have, the most profound is that the German Hitler government bears great responsibility. This crime was instigated and guided by Germany. Can Europe tolerate this any longer? Can Britain, France, and Italy turn a blind eye? Can the League of Nations stand by?" Le Journal reported, "The current situation is serious no matter how you look at it. If the countries' front lines cannot unite after Dollfuss's death, the situation will become critical from serious. But Austrian independence must be maintained, and Italy should take the lead in taking emergency measures, as the Italian troops stationed in Trentino are only a stone's throw away from Innsbruck in Austria. Can the Germans make another mistake?" (Note: Trentino was originally part of Austria, located on the northern border of Italy, but was returned to Italy after the European War.) Le Petit Journal reported, "In any case, all of Europe is already on alert." L'Homme Libre reported, "If we want to avoid a worse situation, emergency measures cannot be delayed." (Havas dispatch, 26th)

German Newspapers' Arguments Are Exceptionally Radical, Saying That the Trampling of Civil Rights Should Cease 63

(Berlin) Today, the more radical Nazi Party newspapers expressed satisfaction with the Austrian incident. One newspaper reported that those who believe they can trample on civil rights to determine their own destiny should take the death of Chancellor Dollfuss as a warning. Another newspaper said that this tragic event should serve as a final warning to Chancellor Dollfuss's comrades, telling them that the time has come to clear out the terror and oppression system. The Berliner Tageblatt said that ambitious and courageous figures have now passed away, and peaceful accommodation is in line with chivalry. These criticisms from the newspapers directly contradict the condolence telegram sent by Foreign Minister Neurath, and it is said that opinions within the Nazi Party are not uniform. (Reuter's dispatch, 26th)

The Soviet Union's Far East Divides New Districts 64

(Moscow) The Presidium of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union issued an order to divide the Far Eastern territory of the Soviet Union into several new administrative regions. The Presidium, in view of the economic and ethnic characteristics of the Far East, ordered the area to be divided into the following administrative regions: the Ussuriysk region, with its center in Nikolsk-Ussuriysk; the Khabarovsk region, with its center in Khabarovsk; the Ruysk region, with its center in Rokelovo; and the Nikiche Molke region, with its center in Nikolaevsk. All districts are directly supervised and administered by the Far Eastern Executive Committee. As for the Kotsk ethnic district, it will be incorporated into the Kamchatka region. (TASS dispatch, 25th)

The United States Denies That the Naval Conference Will Not Discuss Political Matters 65

(Washington) State Department officials today denied claims that next year's naval conference will not discuss political issues. A message from Tokyo claimed that the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs spokesperson said that England, America and Japan had already agreed to this agreement. Previous Tokyo dispatches had promoted Japan's intention to restrict the next naval conference to only discussing naval issues, but the Associated Press today learned from responsible sources that Japan has not yet formally made this request. (National Telegram, 25th)

The Soviet Union Invents Silent Aircraft Cabin 66

(TASS Kharkov communication, June 20) The aircraft factory here is planning to build a high-speed passenger aircraft. The aircraft has two engines, one of which can be removed if necessary, and can accommodate twelve passengers. Its speed is 330 kilometers per hour, and the passenger cabin is very comfortable and silent. This type of silent cabin is being applied for the first time in the Soviet Union.

Exclusive Report

What Happens After the Death of Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss? A Wild Guess 67

(I) The Position of a Little Napoleon

Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss has been assassinated. At this moment, perhaps those political commentators who like to make alarmist remarks will say that this is the second Sarajevo. Whether this incident will lead to a second Sarajevo depends on whether the responsible European politicians deal with it carefully, and whether emotion or reason is the more powerful factor. Intuitively, Dollfuss's death does have the potential to lead to war. If the new government cannot suppress the rebellion, we wonder if France, Italy, and the Little Entente countries will send troops to intervene. If the National Socialist Party fails and retreats into German territory, we wonder if Germany will help these Germanic brothers. We hope that Hitler, Mussolini, and Doumergue will not rely solely on intuition, but we must recognize the seriousness of this incident.

Why does a pocket chancellor, less than five feet tall, have such a large impact on international war or peace? Because he is the representative of Austria's independence. Austria's independence is the center of the Versailles system. The Versailles system is the result of four years of bloody battles, and how many unjust bones and blood have been piled up and dyed to create it. This system needs blood and bones to build, and it takes blood and bones to destroy this system and build another system. Now that Dollfuss has been killed, Austria's independence has become a very serious issue. Those who want to maintain the Versailles system and those who want to destroy the Versailles system are gradually coming into direct conflict. A curtain has been drawn, and whether the play inside will be a martial drama is very worrying.

(II) Dollfuss in the Last Two Years

Dollfuss has been able to maintain his political life for two years because he was happy to be isolated. In foreign policy, he advocated maintaining Austria's independence, and in politics, he has always been a neutralist. When the year of the Republic 21 (1932) came, the Socialists and the right-wing parties attacked each other and could not compromise. His Christian Social Party was composed of conservatives in Vienna and patriots in the countryside. Because he was neither left nor right, he was able to leap from Minister of Agriculture to Prime Minister. Last spring, he turned against the Socialists, dissolved parliament, and at the same time, he not only disbanded the Socialist army, but also searched the headquarters of the National Socialist Party. Last September, he cooperated with the Home Guard, which was a private army that was very reactionary. Dollfuss used them to deal with the left and right wings. Although everyone promoted that this army would revolutionize Dollfuss's life, it has not been realized to this day.

He sought a way out from being attacked on both sides, and the methods he used were very vicious. After Hitler's victory in Germany, the National Socialists vigorously advocated the merger of Germany and Austria, and the National Socialist Party in Germany also helped them in various ways. Hitler's followers used radio broadcasts in Sengcheng to attack Dollfuss's speeches, swaying the psychology of the Austrian people. Dollfuss then arrested the leaders of the National Socialist Party within the country and sought assistance from the League of Nations. Because Austria's existence and the League of Nations' existence are two and one, the three countries of England, France, and Italy jointly declared in February to maintain Austria's independence.

The Home Guard helped Dollfuss clear out the Socialists as a condition, and the Socialists also knew that Dollfuss's dictatorship was not in their favor. On February 12, the Socialists announced a general strike. Dollfuss preemptively destroyed the Socialists' base with artillery and machine guns, killing many left-wing leaders. Those who hated Dollfuss rose up to join the National Socialist Party in an attempt to take revenge. Since reducing the Socialists, he has focused on dealing with the National Socialist Party. On the one hand, he formulated a dictatorial constitution, and on the other hand, he used imprisonment, exile, afforestation, and even execution to suppress the National Socialist Party. This uprising of the National Socialist Party can also be said to be a reaction to Dollfuss's high-pressure policies.

(III) Why Must Austria Be Independent?

Why couldn't Dollfuss die? Because only he can keep Austria independent. Why must Austria be independent? Because once Austria moves, the map of Europe will change color. Austria cannot be independent. In economic terms, its agriculture cannot be self-sufficient, and its industry needs markets elsewhere. Since the Treaty of Versailles, Austria is like a fat man who has been stripped to the bone. Industry is gradually disappearing, and banks are bankrupt. Starting in the year of the Republic 12 (1923), Austria's finances have been maintained by borrowing from the League of Nations. The League of Nations sent a commissioner to Vienna, and all finances were in his hands. If Austria and Germany merge, the two can help each other economically. What's more, the people of Austria and Germany are of the same race and culture. The National Socialist Party wants the Austrian people to let Hitler govern Austria. There is no reason for this.

However, the Treaty of Saint-Germain does not allow Austria and Germany to cooperate. There is even more reason. If Austria joins Germany, Germany will add six million people. The Czech's survival becomes a problem, because in this way, the Czechs are wrapped in Germany. Germany's southern border will connect with Italy, and in the east, it will border Hungary, resulting in Germany being the southern king in Eastern Europe and the Balkans. Moreover, there are three million Germans in the Czech Republic, and most of their residences are adjacent to Germany and Austria. Once Germany and Austria merge, the Czech Republic has no reason to persuade these three million Germans to stay under the flag of a foreign race. But if these three million people rebel and return to Germany, the total population of the Czech Republic, which is fourteen million, will lose a quarter of its population, and its territory will be lost. Can the Czech Republic still be a country?

What's more, there are some non-Czech people in the Czech Republic who have long wanted to break away, such as the 690,000 Hungarians, who are still attached to their homeland. If the Czech Republic loses its existence due to Austria's independence, the map of Europe will be even more different. Among the Little Entente countries, Yugoslavia and Romania are profiting from the Versailles system, and the foreign races within their borders will definitely think of rebellion. The Hungarians will definitely have another "return to the motherland" movement. On the Polish side, because of the Czech's demise, not only will they lose an anti-German assistant, but Germany's opportunity to invade Poland will also increase. Italy has no love for the Versailles system. However, after the Great War, she also obtained the Druer region inhabited by Germans and many coastal territories formerly owned by Austria. Mussolini and Hitler are separated by an Austria, so they are not like-minded friends. Once Austria disappears, the Germans will once again look at Rome across the Alps, which the Italians cannot sleep peacefully about.

Therefore, when Dollfuss dies, Austria's independence is shaken. If Austria is not independent, the new borders of Europe will be like rotten ropes, precarious and about to break.

(IV) How Will the Great Powers Deal With It?

Germany's Hitler is in a position regarding this Austrian rebel party much like Wilhelm II was to the Austrian government when the European War was about to happen. In fact, Germany can control it, and the great powers regard every move of Austria as Germany's order. If we want to ask how Germany will deal with it, we must look at Hitler's position in Germany. Undoubtedly, his position has not been shaken, and he is looking for an opportunity to shift the people's focus to the outside. Domestic failures are often decorated with martial exploits. What's more, with the patriotic enthusiasm of the Germans, they will support their leader if he is tough on the outside.

Italy will not allow the National Socialist Party to take power in Austria. Mussolini has repeatedly declared that Austria's independence must be maintained. We want to ask, if the new cabinet is overthrown and the National Socialist Party takes power, will Italy send troops to intervene? I don't think Italy will take unilateral action, and England and France will cooperate with Italy. The League of Nations is an organization established to maintain the Versailles system, and it must be used at this moment. If Austria is brought to the point of international co-management, it is difficult to guarantee that the National Socialist Party will not start an incident internally. If this thorny problem is not solved with a calm and cautious mind, the result will be chaos.

France and the Little Entente countries undoubtedly want to punish the National Socialist Party. What's more, if Italy is willing to participate, they will gain even more courage. England is also afraid of Germany's expansion, and public opinion will definitely show dissatisfaction with the National Socialist Party's actions, but her attitude will not be as active as France's. At this critical moment, the most noteworthy thing is still Hitler's attitude. If he wants to bet everything on one throw, using the Austrian problem to vent his accumulated anger since taking office, that is a policy of preferring to be a shattered jade rather than a complete tile, and he will definitely be able to gain the support of the German people, but the result is unimaginable. If he is willing to give in, let the League of Nations handle Austria, and let the National Socialist Party be punished, then how long his authority in Germany can be maintained is unknown.

Some say that this uprising of the National Socialist Party is related to Hitler's and Mussolini's previous meeting, or that Italy and Germany have already reached an understanding. However, this speculation has no sufficient evidence and can only be used for reference. (July 26, 9 PM)

Heavy Rain Along the Ping-Sui Railway 74

Rain Mixed with Hail

(Beiping) There was heavy rain along the Ping-Sui Railway last night. The rain in Xuanhua continued all night and was mixed with hailstones the size of chicken eggs. In the middle section, between Fushengzhuang and Sandoying, mountain floods were even more rampant. The new track laid at Qixiaying was swept away by the waves, and the extent of the damage was more severe than before. The areas around Bikeqi in Suiyuan were also flooded. The losses are currently difficult to estimate. The passenger train departing from Zhuozishan to Kaiping this morning is delayed by more than ten hours, according to the Railway Bureau's announcement. (Special dispatch, 26th)

(Beiping) According to the Ping-Sui Railway Bureau, the losses from the two floods are estimated to be more than two million yuan. (Special dispatch, 26th)

The Yongding River Surges Again 75

(Tianjin) The Yongding River surged again on the afternoon of the 25th, with a water depth of 62.75 meters. The dikes in the Pingxi area are low and dangerous, and the southern bank is about to overflow. Wan Pingxian and Men Zhenzhong, director of the Yongding River Affairs Bureau, have gone to investigate. (Special dispatch, 26th)

The Entire Province of Shandong Gets Rain 76

(Jinan) There has been heavy rain from last night to tonight. It has stopped slightly now, but it is still not clear. The provincial government has received reports that the entire province has received rain, and grain prices have fallen. (Special dispatch, 26th)

(Jinan) Han Fuqu reported to Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei that the entire province has received rain for 20 hours, and the autumn harvest is promising. (Special dispatch, 26th)

The Yellow River Has Been Rising for Days 77

(Jinan) The Yellow River in Shaanxi Province rose more than six centimeters on the 25th. Lukou has risen by one meter and four centimeters today, and the upper and lower reaches have also risen. The Shaanxi River will rise again tomorrow. The River Bureau has telegraphed all river workers to take strict precautions. (Special dispatch, 26th)

(Tianjin) Hu Yuanhui, director of the Yellow River Reconstruction Engineering Office in Hebei, came to Tianjin to visit Yu Xuezhong, reporting that the dangers of the Yellow River have been completed, and the Taihang Dam will be completed at the beginning of next month. A total of seventeen kilometers have been rushed to block. The low-lying areas in Puyang are particularly dangerous, so please allocate 2 million in funding. (Special dispatch, 26th)

Proceedings of the Japanese Consular Conference in South China 98

Many Proposals Related to Economy, Culture, and Colonial Industry

Taiwan Governor's Speech Explains the Purpose of the Meeting

Xiamen Correspondence: The Japanese Governor-General's Office in Taiwan convened a consular conference for South China from the 18th to the 20th of this month at the Governor-General's Office in Taipei, the capital of Taiwan. The Japanese consuls attending were Tsukamoto Takeshi from Xiamen, Usami from Fuzhou, Harada from Shantou, Hanbe from Guangzhou, and Ashino from Hong Kong. Hiratsuka, the chief of general affairs of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, served as the chairman (i.e., the presiding officer). The director of internal affairs, the chief of the police affairs section, the director of the education bureau, the director of the colonial industry bureau, and others from the Taiwan Governor-General's Office all attended. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Tajiri, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs sent Araki, and the Japanese Embassy in China sent Yamada to attend. The agenda included items related to colonial industry, education, police affairs, diplomacy, justice, the navy, and the army, indicating deep intentions. According to information from Taiwan, the conference opened at 9:00 a.m. on the 18th. Governor-General Nakagawa attended the meeting, read the imperial rescript on Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, and explained the purpose of convening the conference on the other side of the Taiwan Strait and the attitude towards South China. Then, the various cases were discussed. The conference lasted for three days, and the closing ceremony was held at 5:00 p.m. after the last meeting at 4:00 p.m. on the 20th. The following cases were publicly announced by the documents section of the Governor-General's Office:

(1) Matters concerning the revival of the Foreign Affairs Section of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office (2) Propaganda matters with "Sino-Japanese Friendship" as the guiding principle (3) Matters concerning providing various conveniences to Chinese groups visiting Taiwan (4) Matters concerning the state of coal demand in South China (5) Matters concerning the trade of Chinese canned pineapples (6) Matters concerning guiding the colonial industry of Taiwanese residents and encouraging them (7) Matters concerning the prohibition of smuggling gold ingots out of the country (8) Matters concerning the prohibition of smuggling counterfeit coins into the country (9) Matters concerning the Po Ai Hospital (10) Matters concerning the establishment of a midwifery (female obstetrician) training school at the Po Ai Hospital (11) The problem of concurrently using police officers from the Taiwan Governor-General's Office as foreign ministry police officers (12) Matters concerning the policy for cracking down on opium dens operated by Taiwanese in various parts of South China (13) Matters concerning news articles on the situation on the other side of the strait (14) Matters concerning the operation of the Min Bao (established in Fuzhou) newspaper (15) Matters concerning Taiwanese youth (16) Matters concerning expanding preventive inoculation and treatment for infectious diseases among Chinese people (17) Matters concerning cracking down on those who fail to register as residents (18) Matters concerning cracking down on those who smuggle goods from Taiwan to China on small ships (19) Matters concerning promoting trade between Taiwan and South China (20) Matters concerning providing low-interest loans to support small businesses and matters concerning the connection between local Taiwanese associations and industrial and commercial organizations throughout Taiwan (21) Matters concerning supporting financial institutions for Chinese merchants and Japanese-Taiwanese residents (22) Matters concerning mutual financing among financial institutions for Japanese-Taiwanese residents in South China (23) Matters concerning cultural undertakings on the other side of the Taiwan Strait (24) Matters concerning improving the treatment of teachers (in Japanese schools in China) (25) Matters concerning the broadcasting affairs of the Taipei Broadcasting Station (radio station) (26) Matters concerning adjusting the Osaka Shosen Kaisha shipping company's ships to stop at Fuzhou (27) Matters concerning providing convenience to passengers traveling between Xiamen and Taiwan (28) Matters concerning the expenditure of relief funds for shipwrecked sailors (29) Matters concerning making Chinese customs officials distinguish between shipwrecked ships and smuggling ships (30) Matters concerning simplifying judicial affairs (31) Matters concerning actively assisting the news operated by the Good Neighborliness Association (i.e., the Xiamen Quanmin Daily) (32) Matters concerning mutual assistance among consulates in searching for and arresting criminals (33) Matters concerning notifying overseas residents to register (34) Matters concerning consulates executing the punishment of criminals on behalf of the government (35) Matters concerning the form of arrest warrants (36) Matters concerning cases (37) Dredging the riverbed in front of the Guangzhou warehouse pier (the river refers to the Pearl River) (38) The fixed loan case for the Guangdong branch of the Treasury. In addition to the above, there are also unannounced proposals regarding naval affairs.

The Taiwan Governor-General's Office's convening of this "Conference on the Other Side of the Strait" has temporarily attracted international attention. South China, the Philippines, and the British and Dutch territories in Southeast Asia are all on edge. According to Taiwan Governor-General Nakagawa, who made a statement to reporters after the conference, "The consular conference is easily attracting attention from all parties because it is being held at a time of tense circumstances. However, the consular conference is not as significant or secret as some have claimed. Consular conferences were held twice during the era of Governor-General Tian, but they were interrupted due to the busy affairs of the Governor-General's Office. This time is merely a revival. Regarding Taiwan's policy towards the other side, the basic principle is to enhance the culture between us. Other than that, there is nothing else besides the economic revitalization of the Taiwanese residents and Japanese expatriates in those areas. The operation of social facilities such as hospitals, schools, and news businesses is also in line with the above principle. In order to thoroughly strengthen our opinions, disputes and misunderstandings often arise between us. In order to prevent this from happening, we have each consul come here once a year for various cordial talks, and we will continue to hold them in the future. As a result of this conference, if there is a need for positive measures on the other side in the future, we will increase the budget within the possible scope to promote the 'Policy on the Other Side'," etc. Although the Governor-General's statement is intended to explain the situation, the words are still worthy of contemplation. Tsukamoto Takeshi, the Japanese Consul in Xiamen who attended the meeting, returned to Xiamen on the Guangdong Maru today (the 23rd) after the conference. )23rd(

Japanese Fishing Vessels Investigate Fishing Grounds in Fujian Waters 99

Nets Cast Thirty Times

20,000 Jin of Fish Caught

Xiamen Correspondence: The Guangdong coast in our South China Sea has always been a fish-producing area, but because fishing methods are still old-fashioned, and at the same time the fishing area has been invaded by new-style Japanese fishing boats, the fishing rights in the South China Sea are actually in the hands of the Japanese. Recently, the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry of the government sent the fishing boat Feizhun Maru, with technicians such as Okuma, to the coastal areas of Fujian and Guangdong to investigate fishing grounds. In the area between 114 and 112 degrees east longitude, the nets were cast 19 times, and the total amount of fish caught was about 10,000 jin. In the area between 112 and 110 degrees east longitude, the nets were cast 11 times, and more than 10,000 jin of fish were also caught. According to the investigation results, the area around 112 degrees 30 minutes east longitude and 15 degrees 30 minutes north latitude is actually a densely populated fish area. The fish are mostly of the Banzai red snapper type. Also, about 30 li south of Dajima Island in Penghu Island, a large amount of red snapper fish was also discovered. Fishing boats from the Taichung area go there to fish and can catch 8,000 jin per day. (23rd)

Wuchang County Magistrate Requests Trial of Artificial Rainmaking Method 100

The magistrate of Wuchang County recently submitted a request to the Hubei Provincial Government to imitate the scientific artificial rainmaking method of the United States and Britain to relieve the drought. The original report stated, "Submitting a report for the drought is about to form, earnestly requesting to imitate the scientific artificial rainmaking method of the United States and Britain, trial implementation and verification, and praying for regulations to be established for disaster relief measures after the disaster occurs, so as to promote and rescue, and looking forward to verification and compliance. I, Wuchang County, have suffered a severe flood in the previous year, and the people have been displaced and dispersed, and the vitality has not yet recovered. Following this, the grain prices were low last year, hurting farmers, and the villages are on the verge of bankruptcy. It is heard that the water level of the Yangtze River will increase this year, and all of them are frightened and afraid. However, since the beginning of summer, there has been little rain, the soil is scorched, and the beans and wheat have failed. The county magistrate inspected the villages, and in the space of two weeks, the fields that had already been sown were withered, and the ponds and weirs were dried up, and the view was barren. The disaster of flooding has not been eliminated, and the scorched earth has appeared. All industries are declining, and thousands of households are sighing. The county magistrate is mediocre and disregards the hardships of the people. I believe that the policy of thinking about trouble and preventing it, as well as disaster relief, dare not resign from responsibility. Respectfully, I would like to present what I know for your consideration. In the case of prolonged drought, the traditional methods of disaster relief in our country have always been prayers and prohibitions. In tracing the origin, it is just that the ancient sages and philosophers were expedient measures to calm people's hearts at the time. The intention cannot be faulted, but it is close to superstition and has no basis in fact. It is not to be talked about in the modern world of scientific enlightenment. The county magistrate, in view of the fact that the farmers in our country are bound by ancient methods and have never paid attention to water conservancy, rely entirely on timely rain and sunshine as a standard for abundance, which is not a good plan. In this time of drought, it was initially proposed to try to use water pumps for irrigation. After consulting with President Shao of the College of Engineering of Wuhan University, and after consulting with people in the county, it was considered that each water pump would cost about 30,000 yuan, plus more than 20,000 yuan for a black oil engine, for a total of more than 50,000 yuan. The construction is very expensive, and the fields are not connected or penetrated by ditches, making it difficult to use them all over. Moreover, the county lacks technical talents, making it difficult to design accurately. However, thinking of the many lakes in the county, if there is such equipment, the lake area may be very wide, and at least a part of the relief can be obtained. Unfortunately, due to the limited time and financial resources, even the palliative measures are still not enough to meet the urgent needs. Later, I thought that in June of the 18th year of the Republic of China, Hong Kong suffered from a severe drought and a lack of drinking water. It was reported that the British Governor sent two planes to throw Kaya Lin powder in the air, and it rained after two hours. However, the telex transmission was brief, and there was no academic basis to obtain it. Now, I have checked the magazines published by the China Science Society this year. The 21st issue of the Science Daily contains two kinds of artificial rainmaking methods. One was invented by American scientists Warren and Professor Benkrolo. A large amount of electrified sand is applied and carried to the high altitude by airplanes and scattered in the atmosphere. Soon the rain will fall. According to Professor Peng's estimate, 40 pounds of electrified sand can dissolve one square mile of cloud into rain. The other is Professor Vera's test, using a kind of very fine dry ice, that is, solid carbon dioxide, flown by a single-wing aircraft to 2,500 meters and scattered in the clouds, and artificial rain will fall. The two are very clear in their principles and methods. According to the theory, the trial implementation. The county magistrate follows the habit of the Chinese people. At the beginning of the discovery of a truth, they often scoff at it as nonsense and refuse to test and study it. Therefore, things often lag behind others. The Premier knew it, so he ordered the gist of "Chinese people know the difficulty of doing things" and the saying of "catching up". I believe that this scientific artificial rainmaking method is indeed not baseless. With the convenience of using aircraft in Wuhan, the ease of purchasing chemical raw materials, and the gathering of scientists, it can be verified and tried everywhere. If it is legally used, it will have the effect of a timely rain. If it fails, the loss will be only a small amount of raw materials, and the cost will be very small. Even if no observation is made at present, there will be a day when research will be successful through this advocacy. Moreover, it was reported in December of the 22nd year that some scientists and water conservancy experts in North China, after the Soviet Union invented artificial rain, were also gathering comrades to initiate the organization of an artificial rain research association, saying that they would conduct considerable experiments on both sides of the Yellow Canal, etc. Today, whether this association has been established or not, the details are not known. However, the attention of the people in our country to this research has already been seen. If the government had subsidized and rewarded it earlier, there might have been considerable performance. This is one of the reasons why the county magistrate is not afraid of detouring and dare to make a trivial request. Secondly, if the trial fails, the sky will still not rain, or the rain will not be sufficient, and the disaster cannot be avoided. In order to seek remedies, it is planned to plant late rice and supplement autumn miscellaneous grains, such as buckwheat, corn, autumn beans, vegetables, or other suitable agricultural products. Special promotion and encouragement will be given. As for the lending of seeds and the financing of funds, it will only depend on the Farmers Bank and the Rural Cooperative. This is two things that I dare to ask for and implement universally. Furthermore, when a certain incident occurs, the Chinese people are often flustered and unprepared, and it is too late to plan. After it passes, they forget it and do not take the opportunity to learn from the past and make up for the lost sheep. Therefore, for thousands of years, in the intersection of water and drought, I do not know how many times it has evolved, and there is no thorough prevention method. The county magistrate believes that although the effect of water pumps is great, when the land is red for thousands of miles, even if there are ditches, there is no way to irrigate them. I have heard that the French Southern region has implemented a honeycomb-style stone tower to collect water from the air, and the results are excellent. This method was adopted in the city of Aotou Xiaya on the coast of the Black Sea 2,300 years ago. Now France has made it scientific and more advanced. The principle is to condense the moisture contained in the air into a liquid. The area of condensation into water is 6,000 gallons of water per day for every 1,000 square feet of tower. It can be taken endlessly and used endlessly. Our country can take this as an example. If you order students from this province studying in France or directly entrust our country's embassy in France to conduct on-the-spot investigations, draw patterns, and detail the construction and construction methods, it will not be difficult to order them to imitate this kind of building everywhere. It must be simple and easy to implement. It is not a secret building. The relationship with national defense is comparable. There should be no difficulty in the investigation. This is also a third thing to prevent future droughts, and I dare to ask for the promotion of imitation construction. In summary, except for the second item, which belongs to the county to be able to follow and implement, the other items are compared to empty words and theories, which are of no benefit to the actual situation. I think that theory is the mother of facts. Mussolini said, "Work belongs to everyone, discussion belongs to a few, and decision belongs to one person." All of the above are within the scope of theory. Whether it is feasible or not, please convene experts to discuss it in detail, formulate a plan, and decide to implement it by the provincial government to save the people and benefit the people's livelihood. I am extremely terrified and await orders," etc. (Attachments omitted)

Jiangsu Province Drought Relief and Post-Disaster Work Relief Plan 101

Divided into Dredging Rivers and Supplementing Rural Sidelines

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Shen Baixian, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, went to Beijing to attend the Administrative Yuan's temporary drought relief meeting. He was ordered to draft a work relief plan for the Administrative Yuan meeting's discussion. It is now reported that the Department has drafted a "Jiangsu Province Drought Relief and Post-Disaster Emergency Work Relief Plan," which Director Shen took to Beijing yesterday. It is divided into two parts: A. Water Conservancy Matters; B. Agricultural Matters. The water conservancy matters include six river projects to be renovated and dredged, requiring 15 million yuan. The agricultural matters include building warehouses and supplementing rural sidelines, requiring 2.5 million yuan. The total is 17.5 million yuan, and it is proposed to request the central government to allocate funds for implementation. The plan is as follows:

Water Conservancy Projects (Omitted Above): The drought problems in Jiangnan are not uniform. In the counties downstream of Taihu Lake, the problem lies in the blockage of the tailwaters, with no unobstructed major channels for flood discharge. Moreover, the entrances connecting to the Yangtze River and lakes are mostly elevated. In the dry season, there is no way to smoothly inject water sources. When rainfall is abundant and mountain floods rise together with the rivers and lakes, they overflow and cause major disasters. Therefore, the strategy for governing the eastern part should focus on dredging the Wusong River and building sluice gates at various entrances along the river, with dredging as the most urgent task. The Grand Canal from Zhenjiang to Suzhou is increasingly silted up. The section from Zhenjiang to Changzhou is even more elevated, making it difficult to both store and discharge water. Farmland transportation is also affected. Sluice gates should be built according to the varying elevation of the terrain to raise the water level and deepen the dredging to smooth the water flow. The people along the river have been hoping for governance for a long time and should be implemented as soon as possible. The Danyang and Jintan areas also need to dredge major rivers. The Jiangning, Jurong, and Lishui areas have suffered severe disasters for years due to the silting of Chishan Lake and the blockage of the Qinhuai River. The impact is sufficient to affect the capital. This time, the drought disaster could not be remedied due to the Qinhuai River's dry up. Dredging should be carried out as soon as possible, regardless of the scale of the project. In high-lying areas, the original mountain ponds are all shallow and small. Most of them have dried up this year and cannot draw water. They should be deepened and widened as soon as possible. At the same time, more artesian wells should be opened to increase water sources. This is the governance strategy for the Jiangnan area. This year, the counties along the Tongyang Canal also suffered from drought. Nantong, Taixian, and other counties have all requested relief. The river is an important transportation route in the Lixiahe area. The Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau is now undertaking surveys. It should be dredged together to benefit farmland. In addition to opening ponds and digging wells as local dredging projects, with work funds allocated and handled by each county, about six places should request the central government to allocate funds and raise funds for implementation.

Agricultural Matters: In addition to establishing warehouses, the government should allocate funds to supplement rural sidelines to subsidize farmers' income. The following are the proposed measures and estimated costs: "Building New-Style Warehouses": Among the 61 counties in the province, except for four counties that have already built new-style warehouses, each of the remaining 57 counties should build a new-style warehouse, requiring a total construction cost of approximately 1.57 million yuan. The purpose is to store food and seeds for famine relief and sowing, to handle food mortgages to prevent low grain prices from harming farmers in good years, and to regulate the rural economy. The purchase of grain seeds and mortgage funds will be raised by the local government. "Supplementing Rural Sidelines": (1) Sericulture: "Subsidizing Autumn Silkworm Seed Prices": It is proposed to allocate 160,000 yuan to subsidize seed prices so that the selling price of autumn silkworm seeds can be further reduced by 25 cents per sheet to facilitate promotion. (This province expects to plant about 640,000 sheets of autumn seeds this year. Reducing the selling price by 25 cents per sheet requires 160,000 yuan.) "Establishing a Model Silk Factory": It is proposed to establish a model silk factory in Wuxi, purchase new-style machinery, and study reeling methods as a model for private silk factories. The estimated costs are as follows: A. Building factory buildings, silk reeling factories, silk returning factories, inspection rooms, warehouses, offices, dormitories, and other ancillary rooms, totaling approximately 220,000 yuan. B. Purchasing machinery: multi-position vertical silk reeling machines, 20-end reeling (450 units), silk returning machines (360 units), cocoon boiling machines (3 units), inspection machinery (2 sets), boiler engines, water storage ponds, etc., totaling approximately 220,000 yuan. The total of the above two items is 440,000 yuan. Together with the subsidy for autumn silkworm seed prices, the total is 640,000 yuan. "Animal Husbandry": It is proposed to allocate 200,000 yuan to establish a livestock breeding farm in Zhenjiang to breed a large number of improved breeds of poultry and livestock for promotion. After its establishment, the recurring expenses should be self-sufficient from the production income. "Freshwater Aquaculture": In 25 counties such as Kunshan, an average of 6,000 yuan should be allocated to each county, totaling 150,000 yuan, to develop large-scale aquaculture farms. The estimated cost is 50,000 yuan. ) 26th (

Villagers of Tailiu Township, Songjiang, Robbed 102

On the night of the 24th, in Tailiu Township, which belongs to Sijing Township, more than ten bandits with a Jiangbei accent suddenly broke into the house of villager Li Qiushan through the kitchen door in the southeast corner, each holding long and short firearms, and arbitrarily searched and robbed. The villager's family was not wealthy, and they robbed seven yuan in silver dollars, six dimes in small silver dollars, 6,000 copper coins, and gold rings and clothing, escaping with their loot after about an hour.

Disaster Report from Fuxing Township, Shanyang 103

Shanyang is located near the coast. Recently, due to scarce rainfall, a drought has formed. The Fuxing Township Improvement Association in the area sent a telegram to the county government, stating that there had been no rainfall in the area since the previous day, rivers and lakes had dried up, and the soil had cracked. Rice seedlings were sown in the township at the appropriate time, but due to the severe drought, the unplanted soil was hard and could not be sown, and the planted areas lacked sufficient moisture, resulting in a disaster where everything was lost. A total of 227 households in the township were affected, with 3,055 mu of farmland. They requested that personnel be sent to investigate and that grain taxes be exempted, and that drought relief measures be quickly planned. After receiving the report, the county government ordered the Eighth District Office to investigate and report.

Suzhou Public Security Bureau Bans Temple Fairs 104

In Suzhou, in the past two weeks, the general public has risen up like a swarm of bees to hold temple fairs to pray for rain. The ceremonial guards are changing every day, and the Guanqian Street area is extremely crowded every day. Wang Bolin, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, fearing that it would affect local public order, ordered his subordinates to ban welcoming gods and temple fairs from yesterday (26th). In addition, local gentry Li Genyuan and others had previously invited the Lingguan Guanyin from Guangfu Township to pray for rain, and enshrined it in the Baolian Temple in Sanliuwai. It is now scheduled to be sent back to the township at the end of this month, and a grand farewell ceremony will be held at that time. Since the rain a few days ago, the green seedlings in the fields of the four townships have gradually awakened, but the autumn harvest is bound to be reduced.

Wuxi Cake Shop Owner Commits Suicide Out of Desperation 105

Ren Ahe, the son-in-law of the woman who looks after the Zunxian Temple in Huishan Town, outside the West Gate, used to sell sesame cakes for a living. He had three sons, and the family's expenses all depended on Ahe's support. Recently, Ahe's business has been slow, and his livelihood has been difficult to maintain. He developed a sense of world-weariness and committed suicide by swallowing raw opium yesterday morning. In the afternoon, the toxicity took effect. After it was discovered, Xi Shi immediately called for Western doctor Jin Ziying to treat him, but it was too late. He died at around 3 pm. The local branch reported to the local branch of the 26th Picture (local administrative unit) Zheng Jiang Zixian, and the Shen Prosecutor was sent to inspect the body before it was collected.

The Public Security Bureau's Inspectorate received a confidential report yesterday that No. 22 Hengjie Street inside the West Gate was a well-known organization for selling opium pills. Also, yesterday, the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau arrested Peng Zhang, a known seller of opium pills, and Wu Ashun, a customer, in Chenbaitou Alley. They were all sent to the General Bureau for investigation.

Protection Fees Suspended 107

The local county government, because the protection team's funding was not available, submitted to the provincial government in August last year to levy fees on ships and cars along with tickets, originally for a period of one year. It has been a year since the end of this month. According to the central government's circular, this type of taxation that hinders transportation is also exempted from the list of excessive and miscellaneous taxes. Now, the county government has decided to suspend the levy of all taxes from August 1 this year to reduce the burden on the people. In addition to separate orders, a notice is issued to inform everyone.

Since the drought has caused a disaster, although there has been timely rain, it is still insufficient. Locusts have risen in the four townships one after another, spreading wider and wider. The Drought Prevention Association is still working hard on drought prevention and has purchased 24 water pumpers and five machines. Zhu Fengyuan was sent to the Zhenjiang Garrison Command, and Shen Chenghai was transferred to the Nantong Court. After the prosecutor's investigation, he filed a public prosecution with the criminal court against Shen Chenghai with a life sentence. On the 25th, Judge Long Shiliang tried the case. Zhang Koujiang, a villager in Xinyong Township in the Second District, worked as a peddler. Last winter, he married Mo Jie, the daughter of Yu Lijiang, his eastern neighbor, as his wife. Silk Factories Just Started Work and Will Shut Down Again: Municipal Government Submits Special Request to Central Government for Relief 115

Actively Promoting the Silk Industry to Stabilize Market Prices

Workers Regularly Petition Party and Government Departments

Since the European and American silk markets have been affected by the dumping of Japanese silk, causing the price of Chinese silk to plummet repeatedly, the factories in the city that have started work will shut down again due to unsustainable losses. A reporter from Dagongshe continued to inquire about the recent situation from relevant parties yesterday. The details are as follows:

Implementing Relief 116

Mayor Wu previously received reports from both labor and management in the city's silk reeling industry, stating that the silk industry was in danger and would go bankrupt, and requested that the reports be forwarded to the central government for prompt relief. He immediately instructed the Social Affairs Bureau to investigate the situation of the silk industry and report back for verification. After receiving the order, the bureau has repeatedly convened the silk industry to inquire about the details and has prepared relief measures to report to the municipal government. After receiving the report, Mayor Wu believed that the decline of the silk industry was indeed a fact, and that implementing relief was imperative. He also formulated short-term and long-term measures to save the silk industry and forwarded them to the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Industry for review.

Promoting Sales Abroad 117

In order to fundamentally save the silk industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the Ministries of Finance and Industry have prepared relief measures and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval. However, promoting sales abroad is very important. In the past, the foreign trade of Chinese silk has been controlled by foreigners. Even if some Chinese businessmen operate, they are all weak in capital and have no way to promote sales. In the future, the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces and Shanghai Municipality will cooperate with silk manufacturers and the financial community to organize a Chinese silk sales company. The head office will be located in Shanghai, and branch offices will be established in New York, Lyon, London, India, and other places to enable Chinese silk to be directly exported and sold. At the same time, the situation of domestic silk manufacturers and the rise and fall of overseas silk markets can also be communicated. Regarding these measures, the relevant parties will be responsible for convening relevant parties to discuss them in the near future. If it is deemed necessary to control, various control measures may be implemented.

Stabilizing Silk Prices 118

The silk manufacturers in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai held a joint meeting in Shanghai a few days ago to stabilize silk prices. It was decided to jointly organize an evaluation committee with the financial community, electrical machinery and silk weaving industry, and competent authorities, and Shen Huachen, Jiang Laixian, and Qin Youhe were appointed as external liaison representatives to solicit opinions from all parties. It is reported that the representatives are conducting separate investigations in the past few days. However, since Cai Shengbai, chairman of the Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Industry Association, has left Shanghai on official business, a formal meeting will be convened after Cai returns to Shanghai to discuss stabilizing silk prices and ensure that silk manufacturers can maintain the status quo.

Workers' Petition 119

The silk reeling industry unions in the third, fourth, and sixth districts of the city are deeply concerned that the sharp drop in silk prices has led to indefinite shutdowns of silk factories in various districts, and that the factories that have started work will shut down again, making the livelihoods of more than 80,000 workers precarious. In addition to jointly submitting a request to the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government a few days ago for prompt relief, they have also appointed Chen Xiupu, Yuan Yunlong, Yang Gengti, Yang Shumei, and others to regularly petition party and government agencies. When necessary, they will go to Beijing to petition the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry, requesting immediate relief to prevent workers from taking desperate measures.

The Anhui Rice Merchants Association in Shanghai Requests Postponement of Foreign Rice Purchases 125

Listing Four Advantages and Disadvantages of Ordering Foreign Rice

Please Don't Be Deceived by Rice Merchants in the Executive Yuan

The Anhui Rice Merchants Association in Shanghai has requested the Executive Yuan to postpone the previous proposal to purchase a large batch of foreign rice tax-free, as rice merchants are using drought relief as an excuse, but the provinces along the Yangtze River have had rain in the past month and a bumper harvest is expected. There is no need to order foreign rice. The original text is as follows: To Wang, President of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been dry and the price of rice has soared. The Shanghai Soybean and Rice Industry Association has resolved to take both stopgap and fundamental measures, restricting the price of rice on the one hand and requesting the authorities to order 100,000 shi of foreign rice tax-free on the other hand to avoid high grain prices harming the people. The intention is not bad, but in recent days, most of the provinces along the Yangtze River have had rain and a bumper harvest is expected. The price of rice has fallen. It can be seen that the previous skyrocketing was actually caused by speculation, not a real gap between supply and demand. This is the first point. Moreover, ordering foreign rice is still a matter of raising funds from merchants. If there is no profit to be made, who would make this sacrifice? This is the second point. It is still remembered that a few months ago, there was a request to the government to increase the import tax rate on foreign rice. Now, not only is there a request to order it, but also a request for tax exemption. Once the new grains enter the market, foreign rice will pour in at the same time, and low grain prices will harm farmers. This is inevitable. This is the third point. The intention of ordering foreign rice is to suppress the price of rice. Now the price of rice has fallen, and the new grain will be on the market soon, which is enough to prevent speculators from using their skills. This is the fourth point. The association is engaged in this industry and knows the advantages and disadvantages in more detail. It deeply feels that it is not necessary to order foreign rice at this time, and it is feared that it will deepen the danger of rural bankruptcy. If the harvest is not abundant after the autumn harvest, it will not be too late to order foreign rice next spring to make up for the deficiency. The matter concerns the people's food supply. It is appropriate to report the views as seen above. It is hoped that your seat will adopt it and postpone the previous proposal to order foreign rice tax-free to avoid being deceived by those who seek profit and to prevent the countryside from being hit again. The Anhui Rice Merchants Association in Shanghai bows,

Resolution of the Guang Gang and Taikoo Boycott 126

The Disputes Over Food and Cotton Cloth Lasted for More Than a Year

Both Sides Made Concessions, and Taikoo Paid 30% Compensation

The Export of Xinjiang Vessels Has Resumed Transportation

Since the Guangdong general strike broke out at the British Taikoo Company the year before last, the Cantonese merchants of the grain and cotton cloth gangs have been unable to unload miscellaneous grains and cotton cloth that were stranded in the Taikoo godowns in Guangzhou for a long time, resulting in the spoilage of grain and damage to cloth, and the two gangs suffered losses of more than one million yuan. Later, the two gangs requested Taikoo to compensate them, but Taikoo refused, so the Guang gang boycotted Taikoo ships for more than a year. Now the old case has been re-raised, and the situation has taken a sharp turn. Both sides have made concessions, and Taikoo has acknowledged the losses and agreed to pay compensation. The Cantonese gang has begun to load Taikoo ships. This matter is closely related to the Chinese shipping industry. The situation is described in detail below:

Re-Raising the Old Case 127

The Guang gang's largest businesses are food, cotton yarn, and headcloth. The British Taikoo Company's fundamental business is the Nanhua line. Since the grain and cloth gang's boycott occurred, Taikoo has been affected in transportation. Recently, in view of the fact that the Sanbei Company has opened four new Nanhua special flights, and the four new ships built by the China Merchants Bureau will soon be able to sail to China, Taikoo Company, at the beginning of this increasingly fierce competition, is seeking to consolidate its shipping business and has re-raised this old case of the boycott and proposed to make concessions and negotiate with the grain and cotton cloth gangs to resolve the conditions and end the boycott. With the consent of both parties, they began to negotiate this matter on Monday of this week.

Resolution of the Dispute 128

The yarn and grain gangs had made compensation requests to Taikoo. This matter was first negotiated in Guangzhou and then in Hong Kong. Taikoo considered the amount to be too large and did not agree. Now, they have changed to discussing it in Shanghai. On Monday of this week, representatives of the two gangs and the Taikoo authorities held a long meeting. Finally, both sides made concessions. Taikoo has agreed to pay 30% of the compensation required by the Cantonese gang, and the total amount is said to have reached 270,000 yuan. Yesterday, the reporter asked the Cantonese gang, who acknowledged that this number was correct. The dispute that had lasted for more than a year was brought to an end.

Starting to Transport Goods 129

With the resolution of this boycott issue, Taikoo has notified its branches in various ports to load miscellaneous grains and cotton cloth from the Guang gang. On the Shanghai side, starting from yesterday when the Xinjiang vessel sailed to Guangdong, the Guang gang began to load cotton yarn, headcloth, grain, flour, and other items for export.

This city's Journalists Association, regarding the Nanjing Minsheng Daily being ordered to cease publication by the Nanjing Garrison Headquarters, and its president, Mr. Cheng Shewo, being summoned for questioning and not yet released, yesterday (the 26th) at 5 PM, convened a temporary emergency meeting of the executive committee to discuss rescue efforts. Moreover, Minsheng Daily was not the only newspaper to publish it. Upon investigation, the news item was taken from a news agency dispatch, was inspected by the news censorship office, and was approved for publication. Furthermore, Minsheng Daily was not the only newspaper to publish the news on the same day. This association has carefully reviewed the news item and found nothing that violates the law. Even if it were inaccurate, it could be handled according to the law. However, the authorities have taken drastic measures without following the legal procedures, which seems to be inconsistent with the spirit of freedom of speech and publication under the Provisional Constitution. As colleagues in the same boat, we specially request your review and (promptly inform the Capital Garrison Headquarters) to release Minsheng Daily president Cheng Shewo in accordance with the law to restore his freedom and protect human rights. We earnestly pray. The Shanghai Journalists Association kowtows.
