Reading Q&A

Scientific Rainmaking vs. Praying for Rain (Continued) 197

丨Answer to Zhu Mingjun丨

Zhu Mingjun said that "people in the government and the public" are paying attention to the people's livelihood problems. In fact, "people in the government and the public" may not really be sincerely paying attention to the people's livelihood problems. If we study the current social structure, we will know that in society, some people hope that society will progress and can also promote social progress, but some people try their best to make society backward for their own interests. The movement to cherish the past and superstition is what this group of people is trying to do. Such people are not only in China, but also in other capitalist countries. For example, Japan now has the so-called Buddhist Solidarity Alliance, and churches in Europe and the United States still play a big role in society. These things have a significant effect on turning society backward.

The current disasters in Chinese society are very contradictory: in the Yangtze River basin, drought is caused by lack of rain, while in the Yellow River basin, floods are caused by too much rain. The formation of this contradictory disaster can be said to be a reason for bad weather, but the main reason is social reasons. If there are not so many people in this society who are keen on cherishing the past and restoring superstition, and can try to remedy it with scientific methods like other countries, then the disasters will not be so serious at least. However, it is impossible for Chinese society to use science to remedy it, because scientific remedy must first break all divine power and superstition, and observe nature and society accurately, and then conquer nature and promote society. Such a thing is completely contrary to the interests of some people in society. Therefore, these people would rather stagnate in the superstitious life of 2,000 years ago than allow people to open their eyes to science.

Under the nostalgia of these people, a small number of people are inevitably fooled. However, this deception will not last long, because fantasy behavior will not really benefit the people and will always be exposed sooner or later. Especially those with a little scientific knowledge will not be fooled, nor should they be fooled. We must stand up to passively oppose superstitious actions such as setting up altars to pray for rain, and at the same time oppose the entire nostalgia movement.

The principles of scientific rainmaking will be explained again clearly. (To be continued)

Chunqiu

Imperial Incense Drifting Record 198

— Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

When we were serving her to sleep, we naturally couldn't help but sleep ourselves, but we could only lie on the floor or lean against the wall and doze off with our clothes on. If you were unlucky enough to snore too loudly and wake up the Empress Dowager's good dreams, although it wouldn't be punishable by death, you would be in for an unpleasant time! Whenever it was my turn to work the night shift, I often couldn't sleep soundly. The empty and silent atmosphere of the palace always flooded my mind. I often wondered why the autocratic and unbearable policies that the Empress Dowager was so attached to made Guangxu feel unhappy? The reason was probably because Guangxu was a person full of democratic ideas. The concepts between mother and son were fundamentally different, so of course there was no affection to speak of!

Looking back now, when I was serving the Empress Dowager to sleep in her bedroom, I was formally lying next to her dragon bed, but in reality, I was sitting on the corner of a page of Chinese history.

Those palace maids also had a special car, which was behind the car that the female officials took, meaning it was convenient to take care of each other; however, they had to take care of everything themselves, and no one served them.

We eight female officials had four eunuchs and four servants specially assigned to serve us. They were divided into two groups, eunuchs and eunuchs, and servants and servants. They were lying at both ends of our train car, making our beds every day, preparing water for washing, and sweeping the floor. It was the same when we went and when we came back. However, one thing that made us very inconvenient was that there was no bath to take on the road. Fortunately, this trip was only a very short one, and the weather was not very hot, so we could barely get by. The Empress Dowager usually loved cleanliness the most and took baths very diligently, but it was also very inconvenient to take a bath on the train. She had no choice but to often wipe her body and wash her feet as a substitute. And when she was wiping her body and washing her feet, the train had to be stopped specially. The life of the imperial family is indeed very enviable. Even when traveling on a train, they can still exert their authority as much as possible; but on the other hand, it makes people feel that this kind of life is too rigid, too constrained, and too meaningless. (92)

Tianjin Wei and the Three No-Man's-Land 199

— Sha Jin

In Tianjin, you can often find people wearing hats crookedly, with the collars of their long gowns open, sleeves rolled up, and swaggering around. Just like in Shanghai, you often see people sticking out their stomachs and sticking up their thumbs, saying with a smug air, "Ah, la Shanghai," these people usually have a saying hanging on their lips, saying:

"We are from Tianjin Wei."

Saying Tianjin is nothing: but saying "We are from Tianjin Wei" feels a little different. Yes, its origins are not small.

It is said that Tianjin, the important gateway to the Bohai Sea, was originally called "Haitao" in ancient times and was the place of Jinhai Town in Hejian Prefecture. During the Ming Dynasty, a garrison was established here due to the Japanese pirates, and it was called Tianjin Wei. In the Qing Dynasty, it was promoted from Wei to Zhou, and then to Fu: since the Republic of China, it has been changed from Fu to County: now the names of Tianjin City and Tianjin County exist at the same time. It has undergone many changes, but the name "Tianjin Wei" is still habitually retained, and it is retained in the social group of "We are from Tianjin Wei."

Speaking of this, we want to introduce the Three No-Man's-Land of Tianjin City.

Before talking about the text, we have to sell a gimmick first. I remember a saying, "I am not afraid of heaven, I am not afraid of earth, I am only afraid of speaking official language." This is only "two not afraid." The Three No-Man's-Land is the real Three No-Man's-Land. If you can explain it like this, "The Three No-Man's-Land means that you don't care, he doesn't care, and I don't care either," you understand the Three No-Man's-Land and it counts as pretty good.

Let's get back to the subject.

It is said that this Three No-Man's-Land is where the characters of "We are from Tianjin Wei" gather, and it is also the place where the Chinese Concession, the French Concession, and the Japanese Concession are connected.

Here, there are Go clubs, "Beng Beng Er." Listening to operas, watching movies, and eating pot stickers, drinking Wu Jiapi, all at our convenience.

There are also "flower girls"...

Sometimes, "We are from Tianjin Wei" comes to guest star in a "Slashing Three Passes" or "Killing Cai Yang." It is said that they hurt their harmony because of "Wulongyuan," or that "Li Kui Seizes the Fish" was not friendly enough: and made these "masters" angry and show off their "Spring and Autumn Blade."

In this place, the national heroic performances of these garlic-eating are very worth watching.

Our Kind Neighbors 200

— A Jie

Our kind neighbors, although they cannot compare to the mansion districts such as Jing'an Temple Road and Hess Road, are still quiet lanes, what "villages," what "neighborhoods," the former what "Li," seem less modern than them. There are also patrolmen with guns on their waists at the entrance of the village, and there are also many cars in the village. In the morning and evening, the cool breeze blows on the leaves, there is a lot of rural flavor, and a few pretty ayis often push the sleeping cars of small babies and chat with the male servants of other families. You think! Our kind neighbors are either petty bourgeoisie, or managers of banks and money shops, or compradors of foreign firms. Actually, some of your guesses are wrong.

Neighbor A is an agent in the Gold Exchange. Grabbing hats and cutting flying heads, it is not uncommon to earn thirty or forty yuan a day. He is a young man of twenty-one or two, and he has many girlfriends coming in and out. At night, he either runs to the dance hall, or the handball, or the dog racing. These days, it's hot. After two o'clock, he is still not happy to sleep. He pulls the erhu and hums Beijing opera, very happy. His wife, who seems to be around thirty years old, is very generous and dresses very charmingly. She also smokes a cigarette. This young man bows to her like she is his mother. It is said that since this young man got his wife, his courage to make gold has become more and more powerful.

Neighbor B, some of you may not believe it. It turns out that his house is also full of red sandalwood furniture; radio, bathroom, everything is complete. His occupation is a chauffeur. It is not that the wealthy East Lord gives him special preferential treatment, special high wages, or special extra money. However, the wealthy East Lord's daughter knows the hardship of his job as a chauffeur, especially values him, and especially takes care of him, so that he has established a small mansion for a chauffeur.

Neighbor C's occupation is even more peculiar. He hired two or three money-making partners who do not eat or get paid. Today a monk comes to chant scriptures, tomorrow a Taoist comes to perform rituals, saying it is a hospital, but it is not a hospital. Saying it is a temple, but it is not a temple. Saying it is a warehouse, but it is not a warehouse. But his occupation can cure people's diseases: and can predict good and bad luck; and welcomes ladies and misses to play cards, smoke, chant scriptures and worship Buddha in his home. The partners he hires sit precariously in the hall all day long, without having to do anything, and can earn money for the boss. Isn't opening a "Buddha shop" a good business for the old man to make money?

There is also Neighbor D, who is the sister-in-law of a rogue; Neighbor F, who is an outdated politician who buys short and sells short; Neighbor E, who is a famous Jianghu fortune-teller: loquacious, I don't have the time to write a biography for them, but I lived in the pavilion room for a month, and I gradually became ugly, so I quickly moved away.

Rain and Wind 201

— Shi Ying

Northeast Four Battalion Commanders 202

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 32: Amusements of Sight and Sound, the General Enjoys Himself All Day Long; The Old and Young Weep, Soldiers Almost Return.

Madam Jiang understood in her heart that this must be the division commander. She immediately squatted down to show respect and ensure her legs were safe. Only then did the division commander take out the cigarette he was holding in his mouth, tapped off the ash into the spittoon beside him, and then asked: "What is your esteemed surname?" Madam Jiang said: "My surname is Yang." The division commander said: "Are you also in the grain business?" Madam Jiang said: "My in-laws are in the grain business." The division commander said: "What? Are you related to the grain store across the street?" Madam Jiang said: "No, my in-laws used to manage disaster relief in this grain business." The division commander said: "Are you saying that he gave his daughter to you, or you gave your daughter to him as a daughter-in-law?" Madam Jiang said: "His daughter-in-law is my daughter." The division commander said: "How many daughters do you have?" Madam Jiang said: "Just one." The division commander became agitated upon hearing this, suddenly straightened his back and sat up straight, and asked: "Is she married?" Although Madam Jiang felt that this division commander was being too long-winded, she didn't know why, but she felt timid after arriving at this place, perhaps frightened by the two guards she saw in the alley. So she continued to answer: "She's been married for more than half a year." The division commander said: "What does your son-in-law do?" Madam Jiang said: "He's a battalion commander." These four words entered the division commander's ears and felt particularly uncomfortable, but he couldn't say that your son-in-law shouldn't be a soldier, so he said "Oh," and asked: "He's in the military. Where is he a battalion commander?" Madam Jiang said: "He's been stationed outside Xifengkou, and we haven't heard from him in almost two months. We're very worried. Is it peaceful outside the pass now, Division Commander?" Upon hearing this, the division commander stood up and asked: "Do you know where he's stationed outside the pass?" As he spoke, his eyes were fixed on Madam Jiang's face. Madam Jiang said: "I do know, he's stationed in Ping'an Fort." The division commander suddenly sat back down on the chair. At the same time, the color on his face changed from pale to red, and he asked: "What is your son-in-law's name?" Madam Jiang said: "His name is Zhao Ziqiang. I hope the Division Commander will promote him in the future." (443)

Biographical Sketches

Shanghai Book Collectors in the Qing Dynasty 203

— Shanghai News Agency

Last time when we talked about old Shanghai's book collectors, we issued a reservation coupon, saying that there were other famous book collectors of the Qing Dynasty who would appear in the "next issue." Now we will redeem this reservation coupon.

Qing Dynasty scholarship was shrouded in the atmosphere of textual research, so Qing Dynasty book collectors also had a strong archaeological flavor, proofreading classics and history, researching bronze and stone inscriptions, which was different from the style of book collectors in the Song and Ming dynasties. Shanghai was no exception.

Li Yunjia, styled Xiulin, also known as Sunxiang, lived during the Jiaqing and Daoguang periods. This was the heyday of Qing Dynasty scholarship, and Li was able to follow and match the contemporary talents. He bought the former residence of Zhu Chaqing of the Ming Dynasty, the Ciyun Tower, in the eastern part of the county seat, and collected more than 6,000 kinds of books, which were stored there. In the sixth year of Daoguang, Gong Zizhen wrote a preface to his bibliography, saying, "The Li family of Shanghai has a collection of more than 4,700 kinds of books, with notes and commentaries totaling 390,000 words. The style of peace and prosperity shines together with the Fan family of Yin County, the Wang family of She County, and the Wu and Bao families of Hangzhou for eighty or ninety years." To put the Tianyige, Zhenqitang, Pinghuazhai, Zhibuzu Zhai, and Ciyunlou together, it can be seen that the atmosphere of that day covered the coastal area.

Speaking of Li's bibliography, one admires his academic rigor. He was able to collect books and also able to read them. Therefore, he compiled the books in his collection into an eight-volume catalog, and also included his reading notes in it. He once said: Hui Dongzhu's Yi Dayi uses the Doctrine of the Mean to explain the Book of Changes, which is not the attitude that a Han scholar should have; Jiang Sheng's Shangshu Ji Wangyin Shu changed all the modern characters into ancient characters, which is a bit rigid and unyielding. These opinions are considered to be very accurate.

Li Yunjia's grandson, named Zhongqing, was skilled in poetry, and his collection of paintings and calligraphy included many fine copies, such as General Xiao Li's Spring River Picture, Old Man Shangu's Thousand Character Classic, and Zhang Zeduan's Qingming Shanghe Tu Poetry Scroll, all of which were rare. Qiao Chongxi's poem mourning Yunjia said, "After your death, the collection of books will be scattered." It is unknown whether this was because his son was incompetent or because his son was too young when he passed away. During the Xianfeng and Tongzhi periods, Bao Shuzhi's Baoshu Zaji, written by a native of Ganquan Township, said that the Jin-engraved Kong Family Ancestral Hall Guangji, formerly collected by Li Sunxiang, was obtained by Ma Huzhai, a contemporary.

Mei Yizheng, styled Fuzhai, loved books by nature, and personally collated good editions. Over the decades, he compiled a forty-two-volume collection of books. He was a contemporary of Li Yunjia, but not as famous as Li.

Speaking of the history of book collection in the Qing Dynasty, one cannot avoid the relationship with Suzhou Prefecture. Because in the late Ming and early Qing dynasties, almost all the old books of the Song and Yuan dynasties belonged to Qian Qianyi and Mao Zijin, and were scattered from the two families to Ji Zhenyi, and then returned to Huang Yaopu, and then to Wang Langyuan, and never went beyond Wu "Gate." However, when Wang Langyuan's collection of books was dispersed, a part of it flowed into Shanghai and was obtained by Yu Taifeng. Taifeng's name was Songnian, styled Wanzhi, and he was an En Gong student in the twenty-fifth year of Daoguang. Songnian was rich and fond of reading. At that time, the Taiping Army recovered Jiangnan, and the books in Wu were scattered. Because Shanghai was outside the military area, the Yu family took this opportunity to preserve many old editions. However, his collection of books was soon scattered, and most of it was obtained by Ding Richang. Later, when Ding's books were scattered, a part of them flowed back to Shanghai Hanfenlou (later the Oriental Library).

Xu Weiren, a contemporary of Yu Songnian, was also a great collector and a epigraphist. His name was Wentai, styled Zishan. His appraisal of rubbings was regarded as the best by contemporaries. He once obtained the Dong Meiren Stele from the Kaihuang period of the Sui Dynasty, which was a very rare ancient engraving, so he called himself "Suixuan."

Suixuan paid close attention to collecting local literature. The rare Jiajing Shanghai County Chronicle and the extremely rare Wanli Shanghai County Chronicle were both temporarily housed in the Xu family. (The Wanli Chronicle has a Zhuwen Chang seal that says "Formerly collected by Xu Zishan.") Now the "Jia Chronicle" has been circulated in the form of photo-lithography by the Chuanzhen Society, and the "Wan Chronicle" is stored in the Xuhui Library.

After this era, we should pay attention to the library of group culture. When we recall the magnificence of the individual efforts of the past era, we must express our respect.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Issues Instructions on Key Points for Improvement of Colleges and Universities (7)

Shanghai National Conservatory of Music 204

The students in the training program of the school are diligent and their academic performance is also remarkable, which is commendable. As for the shortcomings of the school, except for the two items of funding and school buildings, which should be addressed after the Ministry plans specific measures, the number of students in the school's specialized departments should be expanded as much as possible, and musical instruments, sheet music, books, and other teaching equipment should be increased appropriately within the possible range. In addition, attention should be paid to the collection of national folk songs and ballads and the research of music teaching materials for primary and secondary schools in Europe and the United States for reference. According to reports, the school has found it difficult to recruit high school graduates due to various reasons, so it can recruit junior high school graduates and extend the length of study to provide relief. The detailed measures should be properly drafted by the school and submitted for approval.

Shanghai Private Fine Arts College 205

The key points for improvement of the school are specially highlighted on the left:

(1) The school's financial difficulties have led to huge debts. In the future, it should actively raise funds. The current assets and debts should be cleaned up and estimated by experts as soon as possible, and a repayment plan should be formulated. The school property should be clearly defined and not mixed with private property. On the one hand, it is appropriate to prevent abuse and compensate for the arrears of salaries to teachers and staff this year. The accounting should adopt new-style bookkeeping and strict management to ensure that what is taken from the students is still used for the students.

(2) The deposit for building a new school building is only more than 10,000 yuan, which is far from enough. Active planning should be made to complete it as soon as possible.

(3) When the inspector went to the school this time, many students were late for the drawing class. It is said that classes start at 9:00 every morning and roll call is at 10:00, which shows that the school's supervision of classes is very lax. In the future, the methods of management and training should be comprehensive, and enrollment should be carefully selected. Students' academic qualifications, grades, and graduation procedures must be reported in advance for approval in accordance with the regulations.

(4) The sculpture department's imitation of antiquities and plaster models is well-intentioned, but the manufacturing should still pay attention to the representative works of art from past dynasties in our country, and at the same time pay attention to the research of decorative arts in our country.

(5) According to the school's outline of organization, the school may set up a research class but not an institute. The research institute should be renamed the research class.

Shanghai Private Xinhua Art College 206

The key points for improvement of the school are highlighted on the left:

(1) The school's funding can only maintain the status quo, and the main source is student fees, which is enough to hinder the progress of school affairs. It is urgent to raise funds to enrich the equipment. The accounting records are not detailed enough, and new-style bookkeeping should be used to thoroughly organize them.

(2) The school building should be actively expanded. It is reported that a part of the existing building is not very strong, and engineering experts should be hired immediately to inspect it to prevent accidents.

(3) Each department of the specialized department is still called a department, which is inappropriate and should be renamed a group. The research institute should be renamed the research class.

(4) Teachers and students often have absences from class, which should be strictly prevented. Teachers should be given higher salaries, and enrollment should be carefully selected. Students' meals should be arranged on campus.

(5) The library only opens after 4:00 p.m. every day, which defeats the purpose of setting up a library and must be revised.

The board of directors and school authorities of the school should pay close attention to the above points and actively improve them.

Suzhou Private Fine Arts College 207

After completing the new school building, the school was able to raise more than 10,000 yuan in the midst of difficulties to increase the equipment of the practical arts department. The efforts of the board of directors and the school authorities are commendable. However, the original operating expenses are very small, which can only maintain the status quo, resulting in no ability to develop school affairs. In the future, it should actively raise funds, expand equipment, increase teachers' salaries, hire more excellent professionals, and increase the number of specialized students to seek the development of the school. The accounting is still using the old-style account book, which is not clear enough and should be replaced with new-style bookkeeping. In addition, attention must be paid to the qualifications for admission during enrollment. The above points should be followed immediately. The establishment of practical arts courses in public and private art colleges has been ordered by the Ministry for compliance. The school has added a practical arts department and has considerable equipment. The management is still practical. Suzhou is one of the handicraft centers in our country. Recently, due to the impact of industrial competition, it has suffered a setback. If the province can use the equipment of the school's practical arts department to jointly run a practical arts vocational school, it will be helpful to the local handicraft industry.

Wuchang National Wuhan University 208

The school's new school buildings have a beautiful environment and are able to pay attention to equipment, which is very suitable for teaching and research. All facilities of the school are in compliance with regulations. The faculty and staff of each college are full-time, the students are diligent and hardworking, and the academic style is good. The law school is particularly able to pay attention to research, which is commendable. However, the following points still need to be improved:

(1) The classrooms of the school's science college lack sufficient light, and the laboratories are also too small. The doors and windows of the dormitory are set against the wall, failing to take advantage of the natural scenery. In the future, new buildings must pay attention to aesthetics, but at the same time, they must also consider the applicability aspect.

(2) The equipment of the school's science college is gradually improving. In the future, if teachers are selected more carefully and teachers are made to devote themselves to research, teaching efficiency will be improved.

(3) The school is a newly emerging university, and the president's duties are heavy. The original position of director of the chemistry department should be filled by another expert to take charge.

(4) The school's engineering college has been established, and its newly established departments should continue to be filled with equipment. The preparations for the agricultural college should be carried out effectively.

(5) The school's training and student coursework should continue to be made the responsibility of teachers to pay close attention to and provide practical guidance, with the overall goal of promoting a simple and orderly academic style and displaying a spirit of enthusiasm.

Wuchang Private Huazhong University 209

Although the school's funding is small, the distribution is reasonable, and the equipment is generally sufficient for application. Most of the faculty and staff are full-time and able to serve enthusiastically. The students are diligent in their studies, and the level is neat, and the performance assessment is also serious. These achievements show the efforts. However, the school's organizational outline lists music groups, mathematics groups, and physical education groups. The nature of these groups is not very clear and should be submitted for review.

(1) The department of social sciences has few students and does not need to be divided into groups. After reviewing the content of the department's curriculum, it should be renamed the department of history and social sciences.

(2) The departments of educational methods, educational administration, and the sub-department of educational psychology should be merged and renamed the department of education, and attention should be paid to the training of teachers for secondary schools.

(3) The mathematics group's curriculum should be merged into the physics department, and the music and physical education groups' curricula should be merged into the education department. Students in the department can still take elective courses, and it is not necessary to call them groups.

In addition, the school's recognition that graduates from Wenhua Middle School and other 13 schools have priority in taking the entrance examination is also inappropriate. In the future, open recruitment should be conducted, and graduates from public and private secondary schools registered with the Ministry should be treated equally. The school should also appropriately increase the number of domestic specialized scholars to teach political, economic, social, and historical courses.

Wuchang Private Zhonghua University 210

The founder of the school is quite intent on developing school affairs, but the financial resources are limited and the management lacks achievements. It should immediately follow the following points and make practical improvements to facilitate rectification:

(1) The school's original school site is not suitable. Although it has been added over the years, the land is small and the houses are many, and there is almost no space in the school. Safety, hygiene, practicality, and aesthetics have not been taken into account. It should raise construction funds as soon as possible and build the Dongshan school building as soon as possible, and move the university part out. The primary and secondary schools should still be run separately at the original site.

(2) The school's funding is far from the standard stipulated in Article 10 of the University Regulations, and the source of income is not stable. Recurring expenses still require borrowing, and there is no mountain plan for construction. A foundation should be added to thicken the economic foundation.

(3) The school's financial resources are limited. It is not enough to allocate them to the original colleges and departments, as well as the primary and secondary school departments. The scope should be reduced and the content should be enriched. The chemistry department should be discontinued immediately, and students in the department may be ordered to transfer to the physics department to continue their studies, or find ways to transfer to other schools to study or borrow classes. Other departments should submit a reduction plan to the Ministry for review within one month from the date of the document.

(4) There are very few books in the school's library that can be used for teaching reference. Books on mathematics, physics, and chemistry, as well as important scientific journals, are particularly rare. The equipment for ordinary physics experiments is insufficient for application, and the equipment for advanced experiments is lacking. Chemical instruments and reagents are also extremely lacking. All of the above equipment must be added as soon as possible to facilitate teaching. (5) Some of the school's directors and professors lack expertise in the courses they teach and hold concurrent positions outside the school, which greatly affects teaching efficiency. Specialized talents should be hired as professors as much as possible to teach earnestly.

(6) The school has recruited new students in the past with too low standards, and the grading of usual exams is also too lenient. There are no strict regulations on repeat grades, suspension, and other punishments, so that students neglect their studies and their levels are low. In the future, the standards for recruitment must be raised, and the entrance examination must be strictly administered to reduce the number of admissions. After admission, the courses must be checked carefully, strictly trained, and strict rules must be established and implemented.

Hubei Institute of Education 211

The institute's teachers, equipment, and curriculum are not substantial, and other management conditions are mostly unsuitable. Enrollment should still be suspended this year. The existing classes should reduce education subjects and increase natural science and agronomy courses. The fundamental improvement measures of the institute should be drafted separately by the department and submitted for review.

Anqing Provincial Anhui University 212

The school should strive to improve the key points for improvement are as follows:

(1) The mathematics and physics departments of the College of Science should be merged into the department of mathematics and physics.

(2) The law school will be closed immediately. The original students will either be allowed to transfer to another school or be allowed to change departments. The school will draft measures for handling it.

(3) The establishment of the College of Agriculture should begin with equipment. In the future, it must be approved by the Ministry after inspection before enrollment.

(4) In addition to complying with the Ministry's enrollment restriction order this year, the number of students in each department should be reduced in the next academic year, and the entrance examination should be strictly administered.

(5) Teachers should be full-time in principle, and part-time teachers should be reduced as much as possible, not exceeding one-fourth of the total number of teachers. The number of teachers should also be reduced effectively.

(6) Rules should be established to strictly limit teachers' absences from class and students' absences from class.

(7) Equipment fees should be increased as much as possible, adding books and instruments, and building school buildings. This cannot be delayed any longer and should be carried out as soon as possible.

Changsha Private Xiangya Medical College 213

The school is able to strictly implement training, management, and teaching, which is commendable. Other management conditions are generally not unsuitable, but the school's source of funding is not stable, and a fixed fund should be raised separately and the content should be enriched.

Tianjin Private Nankai University 214

The school's teachers are strictly full-time and able to work hard in teaching. The internal management of the school is also effective. The economic research association, the chemical industry research institute, and the department of mathematics have rich collections and have made considerable achievements, which are commendable. However, the following points still need to be improved effectively:

(1) The curriculum and teachers of the school's economics college and business college are almost identical, and there is no name for the economics college in the university organization law. The economics college should be canceled immediately, or it should be merged with the economic research association and reorganized as an economic research institute, which should be submitted for review separately. The original departments of the economics and business colleges should also be considered for reduction and merger and submitted to the Ministry for review.

(2) The pre-medical department of the school is not in accordance with the Ministry's regulations. The pre-medical course has long been canceled by the Ministry's order. The department should be discontinued immediately, and the original students should be allowed to transfer to other departments of the College of Science.

(3) The school's physics department should hire excellent professors to be responsible for guidance, so that it can develop evenly with other departments.

(4) The names of all courses in the school's curriculum are in English, which is also inappropriate. In the future, they should all be changed to Chinese.

Hebei Fisheries College 215

The points that the school should improve are ordered separately as follows:

(1) Suspend the recruitment of specialized students (new students and transfer students) from the next academic year.

(2) The attached senior vocational fisheries department should be renamed the attached senior vocational fisheries school. The curriculum should be compiled and organized in accordance with the provisions of the teaching subjects and time summaries of the vocational school departments promulgated by the Ministry.

(3) Actively find ways to move the school to the coast.

(4) Make a reasonable allocation of the original funding and seek to increase funding, enrich equipment, reduce the number of staff members, and hire specialized talents.

(5) Find ways to establish contact with fishermen along the coast near the school, and organize vocational training classes at appropriate coastal locations to impart fisheries knowledge and promote the improvement of fisheries or fishing.

(6) Whether to resume the recruitment of specialized students in the future will depend on whether items 3 and 4 can be realized.

Ministry of Education Handles Schools with Poor Exam Performance 220

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 26th) The Ministry of Education has telegraphed provincial and municipal education departments, ordering that any public or private middle schools with excessively low exam scores, or those deemed weak in performance after inspection, should have their enrollment restricted or suspended. They are to be ordered to improve within a specified period. Those with severely poor performance and deemed unlikely to improve should be ordered to close down.

The summer military training for high schools and above in this city has concluded for the first batch of schools. Shanghai Education Association Eager to Recover Education Rights in Concessions 222

Requests the Education Bureau to Form a Special Committee to Design Improvements

And Sends Letters to Various Organizations and Schools to Advocate Unanimity

In order to recover educational rights in the concessions and advance the overall education of Shanghai, the Shanghai Education Association, after its board of directors passed six measures to improve education in the concessions (already published in various newspapers), has specially requested the Municipal Education Bureau to organize a special committee to design improvements to education within the concessions. It has also sent letters to the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession and various organizations and schools at all levels, urging them to strive together. With this in mind, our association specifically resolved six measures to improve education in the concessions at its twenty-seventh board meeting. In addition to submitting a request to the Shanghai Education Bureau and sending letters to various legal organizations to strive together, we are also forwarding a copy of the measures along with this letter. We sincerely hope for your support and vigorous promotion to achieve these measures, for which we would be deeply grateful.

Various Organizations Prepare to Welcome Him Back

Speaking of Progress in Educational Construction in Jiangxi Province, etc.

The important bandit areas that have been recovered are now being developed with full effort, with remarkable achievements. The annual meeting, under the guidance of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, was extremely successful. The various proposals discussed were particularly practical.

Hangzhou Women's Vocational School 233

Hangzhou Women's Vocational School has been operating for more than 20 years, and its graduates have served in society all over the country. Minhua Vocational Middle School 234

Wins the Right to Challenge for the Cup

(London, 25th, Reuters) The American Davis Cup tennis team, today, in an extremely dangerous situation, turned danger into safety, eliminated Australia, and won the right to challenge for the cup. They will compete with England on the 28th, 30th, and 31st for the right to challenge for the cup.

On the first day, the United States lost two singles matches to Australia. Shields lost to Crawford, 6-1, 6-2, 12-10. Wood lost to McGrath, 7-5, 6-4, 1-6, 9-7. The United States won 3-2 and won the right to challenge for the cup. The results are as follows:

Wood (US) 6-3, 9-7, 4-6, 4-6, 6-2 Crawford (Aus) Shields (US) 6-4, 6-2, 6-4 McGrath (Aus)

Wood Wins Crawford After Hard Fight 236

Many spectators watched today as the match between Wood and Crawford continued. Crawford had the upper hand everywhere, and various different strokes, cross-court shots, and sideline shots made it difficult for Wood to cope. After Wood lost the third set, he fought back bravely in the fourth set. In the third game, after nine deuces, Wood finally won the service game, but Crawford still won the set in the end. In the final set, Wood completely regained his championship form, defeating Crawford with low and accurate angled shots.

Shields Wins McGrath 237

Shields defeated McGrath easily. His terrible serve put him ahead 4-1 in the first set, and he won 6-4. McGrath was completely unable to perform as he had when he defeated Wood, sending extremely easy balls into the net. McGrath fought desperately in the final set, tying the score at 4-4, but ultimately failed to withstand Shields' cannonball serve and lost.

Free Talk

On the Theory of Literary Ventilation (Part 1) 245

— Chen Youqin

If there is oppression, it is natural to release it quickly. One cannot live without oppression, and oppression cannot be left unvented. This is almost universally felt. The heart should go out for a spin, being locked up indoors all the time isn't the way to go. But while everyone desires to release oppression, the ingenuity of the methods varies from person to person. The best at releasing oppression is the literati; the worst is the fool, because the fool's "cursing the undertaker" is not a "skillful" or "ingenious" method. (Someone translates "Humour" as "the marvel of words.")

Chu Ch'i-pai believed that literature is a "symbol of suffering," but I believe that the release of suffering must be the essence of literature. Ordinary literati have four methods of venting oppression, and "cursing the undertaker" is not one of them. Jiao Da's complete revelation of the ugly state of the Grand View Garden is ultimately not a clever approach. Since literati cannot learn from the *Book of Changes* to "escape the world without oppression," they must find ways to vent the oppression they see and feel. The method of venting must both open the appetite and please the eyes and ears. This is why humorous literature is so popular in this era. I fundamentally do not understand what humor is, but I love to talk about the methods of venting oppression by literati. What are the four methods of venting oppression? First, satire; second, implication; third, coldness and refinement; fourth, indignation.

Now let's talk about the first method of venting oppression, satire. Confucius said, "There are five ways to advise, and I follow the way of satire." If the mouth must offer advice, the heart must already be suffering. To vent this suffering, one must not be direct or rude. The best way is to start with satire. Poets use the image of large rats eating millet seedlings to satirize rulers who heavily tax the people. Zhu Xuhou's field-plowing song uses the phrase "those who are not of the same kind should be weeded out" to subtly imply the elimination of those not of the royal lineage. Cao Zijian's seven-step poem uses the metaphor of "cooking beans with beanstalks" to satirically advise his elder brother not to persecute him. As for disliking someone without directly criticizing them, but dusting flies with a fly whisk and saying, "Where did you come from? Why do you gather here!" More of these examples can be found in *A New Account of Tales of the World*. Other examples, such as the writings of Zhuangzi and Mencius, Aesop's Fables, and Liu Zihou's "Three Admonitions," are all good examples of satire and can be considered the champion of methods for venting oppression.

The second is implication. The effect of implication is that the listener must think about it to understand. His oppression is vented without being vented, and this is the most flavorful. The best at venting oppression through implication can be found in the words of lyricists:

"When young, I knew not the taste of sorrow,

I loved to climb the tower,

I loved to climb the tower,

And forced myself to write poems about sorrow."

"Now that I know the taste of sorrow,

I want to speak, but I stop,

I want to speak, but I stop,

And instead say, 'It's a good autumn day, it's getting cool!'"

What a great "It's a good autumn day, it's getting cool!" After "I want to speak, but I stop," there is endless oppression being endured. Although he only says five words, "It's a good autumn day, it's getting cool," people already know that he is full of complaints. This is what Sikong Tu meant by "Without a single word, the elegance is fully captured. The language does not involve oneself, yet the suffering is unbearable." Confucius said, "I want to be silent." Buddha said, "Unspeakable! Unspeakable!" Laozi said, "Cannot be spoken of, cannot be named." All these are the same principle! (Note that I am not advocating the unity of Confucianism, Buddhism, and Taoism.)

Later generations of literati who were able to grasp this method of venting oppression through implication are not many. In the poems of the Tang Dynasty, Chen Ziang's "Before, I saw no ancient people; after, I see no future people. Thinking of the boundlessness of heaven and earth, I am saddened and weep," with only twenty-two words, is the best "nostalgic" poem of all time, simply because there is not much ink used, and it has the charm of implication. Just think of the spirit he had, encompassing all the sorrows of the ages in his chest, gently uttering them, and it became a masterpiece for venting the great oppression of the world. Li Bai's "The beautiful woman rolls up the pearl curtain, sits deeply, and frowns. I only see her tear-stained face, but I don't know who she hates." He did not reveal the beauty's heart in its entirety. He only wrote a question, but it has already become the best "complaint of a woman in her boudoir" for thousands of years. The message of high-quality literature can be found in this, not in saying a lot of nonsense.

There is also a wonderful example, seen in a certain novel, which is also for venting a daughter's anger. Not long after Qinchun got married, her husband went away on a long trip. She told of her experience over the years, saying: "At eighteen, I married my husband, at nineteen, my husband left, at twenty, he did not return, and this year I am twenty-one!" There is no fleshy talk like what young poets say now, such as "The fire of youth is burning, the spring of a loving heart cannot be closed," etc. However, the implied meaning is enough for you to savor. Without saying oppression, the oppression is naturally vented. Isn't it better than venting oppression and making people not feel the oppression?

New Ideas of Politicians 246

— Bo Han

The Pan-Pacific Buddhist Congress has already demonstrated the cooperation of China, Japan, and "Manchuria."

Amid the cries for help in the face of drought, Chinese Buddhists and Zhang Tianshi are displaying their supernatural powers. In the provinces of Hunan and Guangdong, which are threatened by banditry, the revival of Confucianism is also in full swing.

On the Pacific coast, where explosives are buried everywhere, religious figures are in the limelight this year.

It is said that politicians used to regard the separation of state and religion as a progressive idea, but recently, for some reason, they regard the separation of politics and religion as an old idea and instead want to combine politics and religion. Not only that, but education and religion should also not be as separate as before.

Their own explanation is this: Last year, Japanese Prime Minister Saito and other cabinet members said at a reception of the Buddhist Federation: "The task of stabilizing people's hearts and guiding their thoughts depends on religious figures." Also, at the previous Japanese Religious Congress, the Minister of Education gave a speech saying: "How can we eliminate the social unrest that modern world suffers from? Although the reasons are complex, tracing back to the root, the emphasis on materialism is the root cause. All social facilities, although they are not ineffective as symptomatic treatments, but as for radical solutions, the overcoming of materialism must be the first. And the overcoming of materialism can only hope for the high tone of spiritualism… The ultimate point of spiritualism must be left to the power of religion." (See *Kaizo*, May issue of this year)

Chinese religious promoters probably have the same view, needless to say. The ideas of the new era should always be equally new.

In short, the idea of defeating Western materialism with Eastern spiritualism is very old and very popular. I wish the victory of spiritualism! || Because the victory of spiritualism is Eastern, and we belong to the East!

But there is one question: does Japanese imperialism want the victory of spiritualism or materialism in Manchuria?

Yes, in the face of their vulgar pursuit of materialism, we can only overcome it with the high tone of spiritualism!

Dear Miss Fei, let me teach you how to jump rope.

— Chen Ming

On Fierce People 247

— Tian

In Cantonese dialect, "fierce people" refers to millionaires or those who possess a large number of soldiers.

But according to those who are slightly thoughtful, the fierceness of fierce people is actually as soft as cotton. The meaning of fierceness is strength, bravery, and vigor. Millionaires and warlords lack these virtues. Is there a millionaire who does not love money? Is there a warlord who is not afraid of death? Are they fierce? They are not fierce!

So, who can be considered a fierce person?

A fierce person generally has a great soul, a strong virtue, residing in a healthy body. Further analysis of this personality can reveal several characteristics:

The greatness of the soul lies in its clarity, which may be innate or honed through suffering. The best metaphor is "light," round and fixed, illuminating all darkness. All the ghosts and monsters of the world are clear at a glance. No matter what kind of hooks or probes, they cannot penetrate the depths of this soul. Although this clarity is seen, its boundaries are unknowable.

Therefore, they regard space and time as nothing. They do not take life as pleasure or death as suffering, nor do they crave life or regard death as a return. They see a hundred years as a moment, yet they can persevere to the end of their lives, seeing a hundred years as a hundred years. They do not distinguish between grand mansions and burial mounds, and they treat wealth and poverty with indifference.

Then, after emptying life and death and worldly laws, doesn't it seem like they are carefree, without self or others? Not so. Although they regard the so-called fierce people of today as children, they are not bloodthirsty and do not drink the blood, sweat, and tears of mankind. They pity all the fools who are dominated by money and fame in this world, planning for their future and relieving the suffering of their souls and bodies.

Using this yardstick to measure the so-called great men and celebrities of ancient and modern times, one can gain new understanding.

Darkness 248

— Ji Qun

It was probably around midnight, because I couldn't sleep, I climbed out of bed, opened the window, and looked at the night scene outside.

Not only was there no moon in the sky, but not a single star could be found. Outside the window, there was only a kind of gloomy, pitch-black night.

In this terrifying darkness, I heard the mournful cries of little birds calling for help and the fierce cries of cruel owls. Afterwards, the air became deathly still, which was truly frightening. Chickens didn't crow, dogs didn't bark, and all the insects seemed to be suppressed by the terrifying, gloomy, pitch-black night, afraid to make a sound, afraid to breathe.

At this time, the only thing that could be seen was the shadow of the bat, neither bird nor beast, daring to fly boldly, proudly, and arrogantly along the corners of the walls and eaves.

"Oh! This is the epitome of the 20th-century world!"

I was ashamed and disgusted by the ugly state of the two-faced arrogant bat, and I hated the sound of the cruel owl.

Oh, darkness! The world is no longer a world. Don't drag on any longer! Heaven, oh heaven! Please brighten up quickly. Sun, oh sun! Why haven't you come out yet? (Written in the mountains of Chaling)

Hometown 249

— Lü Shaoguang

It was the time when the wheat was about to turn yellow. Driven by the whip of unemployment, I was forced to return to my hometown, from which I had been separated for ten years. My wandering heart stirred up endless melancholy in silent contemplation! The Guanyin Temple at the entrance of the village no longer echoes with melodious chimes. The prosperity of incense in the past has vanished with the waves of famine. The winding pebble streets are lined with piles of cow dung, pig excrement, and garbage. The village at night is frighteningly quiet. The watchman's clapper sounds sparsely, like the inner throbbing of the impoverished. In the distant wilderness, there is the faint sound of village women summoning souls, the mournful sound stream filled with fear and sinking into depression! The playmates of my childhood all feel the pinch of life now. When we meet, no one has the heart to mention the laughter of the past. The suffering before our eyes is enough to endure. Alas, my hometown, from which I have been separated for ten years, has evoked a string of personal sorrows!

I Come from the East (8) 250

— Xingye

The border between Canada and the United States stretches for over three thousand miles. If there is a peaceful and ideal national border in the world, this three-thousand-mile border would be the first. For over a hundred years, no conflicts have occurred on either side of the border, and there are no defensive installations on the border itself. Geographically, the United States and Canada are naturally one. Decades ago, ambitious figures in the United States often had attempts to annex Canada by force or diplomacy. Now, such plans are rarely mentioned. Sixty years of goods exchange, economic cooperation, and people-to-people exchanges have made Canada, in effect, a part of the United States. Formally, Canada flies the British flag; economically, they use American goods, read American newspapers and magazines, and follow American customs and trends. Britain's influence in Canada is gradually being replaced by the United States. Of course, the British Conservative Party and the pro-British faction in Canada, since the Ottawa Conference, have used forced measures to increase the interdependent relationship between Canada and Britain, but the voyage from London to Montreal takes more than a week, while it only takes a few hours from New York to Montreal. The Canadian people living on this long, three-thousand-mile border can often greet residents within the US border from their doorsteps. This relationship makes Canadians feel that Washington is closer and more intimate than London.

Commercially speaking, Canada is the United States' largest market. In the past year, Canada's total population of only ten million consumed US$232 million worth of American goods. At the same time, the United States is a major customer for Canadian goods. Last year, Americans bought US$184 million worth of Canadian goods. Moreover, the economic relationship between the two countries is further strengthened by investment. There are now 4.1 billion American capital in Canada, while British capital in Canada is only 2.2 billion.

In terms of transportation and shipping, Canada and the United States are even more interdependent. The two major railways that are the lifeblood of Canada (CPR and CNR) often carry goods and passengers from the United States. In particular, the shipping company Changxing Company (C·PR·) that goes to the Far East does most of its business with Americans. The company's branches are set up in larger cities in the United States. The company's shares belong to people in Canada, the United States, and Britain. The company's business is largely handled by Americans. Changxing Company's propaganda skills are very famous. Every year, many American tourists send money to Canada, mostly as a result of this company's propaganda. However, propaganda must also have practical value as a foundation. Changxing Company's trains, hotels, and ships are indeed cleaner and neater than the American average. And the scenic areas operated by Canadians are also better than those in the United States.

Sudden Rise of Selling Pressure in the Gold Market 252

丨Decline of Five Yuan and Three Jiao丨

The gold market was initially calm but then weakened, due to the sudden deterioration of the situation in Germany and Austria, which impacted people's confidence. The gold market initially opened with overseas silver markets showing stability in England and rising prices in America. The five-gold exchange's forward silver price remained unchanged and slightly decreased by eight haos. London spot gold rose by half a penny, exchange rates slightly decreased, American wheat rose by 1.625, American cotton rose slightly, and stock prices both rose and fell. Preliminary trading opened steadily and then reported stability. After opening, the bank's appetite decreased, and sellers became active and prices went downstream. But the situation was generally stable. The HSBC exchange rate posting was revealed, and the British and American rates remained unchanged, hovering around one yuan, showing a mediocre trend. Later, buyers became more enthusiastic, and prices rose briefly. However, the bank continued to supply, making it difficult to sustain, and trading in the market became more idle and quiet. Later, news came from the Seattle night silver market reporting a decrease of .125, no change, and a decrease of .25, only a slight rebound. The bank continued to sell forward US dollars, and prices went downstream again but the trend was peaceful, merely hovering. After the noon close, a sudden selling trend emerged, due to a Reuters report that the Austrian Chancellor was assassinated and various countries were extremely uneasy. Prices broke the 90-yuan mark. Afterwards, the Seattle night silver market reported increases of .25, .25, .25, and .125. Reuters reported that the situation in Germany, Austria, and Italy was deteriorating. The German Chancellor and the ambassador to Austria rushed back to Berlin, and Italy stationed a large army on the border. The situation in various European countries was expected to become serious. Local sentiment believed that this could trigger an international war, and the market immediately fell. After the official opening, there was still a downward trend, but HSBC aggressively bought sterling, and buyers became active at lower prices. Rumors of Large Imports of Foreign Flour

Sharp Drop in Flour and Wheat Futures 265

After the flour market opened in the morning, the prices for all months showed a sudden downward trend. The price of foreign wheat in Chicago improved by about five jiao, and in Canada by about four jiao. However, after the opening prices, the market suddenly turned bearish. Faced with soaring prices in recent days, various mills were eager to sell, and these solid offers attracted the attention of speculators. At the same time, rumors circulated that the government's borrowed flour, about 600,000, would be imported soon, which worsened the situation. Near and far contracts all declined, and after the second session, due to heavy selling by long positions, the decline intensified. Near and far contracts all fell by three to four fen. After the fourth session, the trend stabilized. Customer demand was still active, and rumors about imported borrowed flour were denied by relevant parties, which stabilized long-term sentiment. However, short-term positions continued to be unwound, leading to a weakening trend. Total daily trading was chaotic and exceeded 1.8 million packages, showing the madness of speculation. As a result, this month's contract fell by three fen, August fell by 1.5 fen, September fell by 0.5 fen, October remained unchanged, November fell by 1.5 fen, and December fell by 1.25 fen.

After the wheat market opened in the morning, the prices for all months showed an initial flat trend followed by a sharp decline. The price of foreign wheat in Chicago improved by about five jiao, and in Canada by about four jiao. Initially, the market was stable, but by the time the August contract opened, the flour futures market had already changed. The recent decline was quite sharp, which led to a loosening of wheat prices as well. Then, major long positions were unwound, causing the market to fall rapidly. The market has been extremely chaotic recently, with foreign wheat falling but local wheat rising the day before yesterday, and foreign wheat rising but local wheat falling yesterday. The fluctuations are irregular and purely driven by speculators. As a result, this month's contract fell by three fen, August fell by five fen, September and October fell by eight fen, November fell by nine fen, and December fell by eight fen. Spot wheat sales remained smooth, reaching over 30,000 packages. Bids from various firms fell slightly by three to four fen, mostly through direct trading by brokers.

Summer Asphalt Sales Smooth, Cold and Desolate 271

Summer is usually the off-season for asphalt. However, in the last ten years, soap factories have provided a market, so it is not completely deserted during the hot season. But this summer is like the situation ten years ago. Because butter, coconut oil, and other products can also be used to make soap, and their prices are lower than asphalt, asphalt has been completely defeated by them. Therefore, the asphalt market this summer can be described as clean as a whistle. Although inventories are reported to be thin everywhere, sales rely entirely on candle-making. Once candle production stops, almost no one cares about the market, and the market is weak and uninspired. Details from Hankou in recent days also indicate that sales have stalled. Local brokers have very little inventory, and the only thing that supports the market is small soap factories, with only 20-30 deals. The selling price is 16.64 yuan per dan for Chongjing, about 16 yuan for Pingjing, 15.24 yuan for Macheng oil, and only 15 yuan for customer oil from Jiangxi and other places.

Snow Pagoda Long No. 120 B 360 yuan, Snow Pagoda Long No. 120 C 345 yuan, Snow Pagoda Long No. 150 B 380 yuan, Snow Pagoda Long No. 150 C 360 yuan.

The Shanghai Silk Factory Industry is in Imminent Danger 274

(Most Silk Factories are Preparing to Stop Work) After spring cocoons entered the market this year, silk sales by foreign firms in Shanghai showed activity, and the price of Grade B white factory silk once rose to over 500 yuan. However, the cost of new cocoons was only 470-480 yuan per bale. Silk and cocoon merchants profited from this, and many rented factories to start processing new cocoons. However, this was short-lived and soon crashed. European and American markets were dumping Japanese silk at low prices, causing the price of Grade B Shanghai white factory silk to fall to 412 yuan per bale. Currently, most of the 33 silk factories operating in the city are short-term operations or processing for others. Their leases are only for three to four months. Due to the lack of buyers for stored silk, each factory reels an average of two dan of silk per day. If sold at current market prices, each factory would lose over 100 yuan per day. It is impossible to sustain this, so they have to sacrifice the rent and prepare to stop production. Over ten factories are expected to stop work by the end of this month.

(Stagnant Sales of Yellow and White Waste Silk to England) High-quality waste silk from China (such as yellow and white long-fiber waste silk, hand-pulled waste silk, etc.) is popular among British firms. After new cocoons entered the market this year, Japanese waste silk (i.e., silk waste) was dumped in England at low prices, causing the sales of Chinese waste silk to England to decline daily. Yellow and white long-fiber waste silk has rarely been exported recently. The last two postal ships, Lan Zhi and others, did not carry any waste silk to Bombay and England.

(Extremely Sluggish Sales of Silk in Europe and America) Overseas raw silk markets are seeing continuous dumping of Japanese silk, and factory sales have stalled. Silk prices in New York, Lyon, and other places are gradually decreasing. The Shanghai silk market shows no sign of improvement, and the market is extremely sluggish. Yesterday, only European firms took advantage of the low prices to replenish stocks, with Yi He and others purchasing 40 bales of dried silk, but this was not a formal market transaction.
